Q:- how to instll packages in kali/debian
by two ways :- hard and easy

1-hard way
  search google ( debian Wheezy package_name )
  sure that it  is wheezy not sequeeze of jessie or sid
  then select select i386
  then download
dpkg -i  new_package
emacs  /etc/apt/sources.list
then add to update in future
deb http://ftp.de.debian.org/debian wheezy main


2-easy way

emacs  /etc/apt/sources.list
then add to update in future
deb http://ftp.de.debian.org/debian wheezy main

apt-get install new_package

air_start(){
airmon-ng check kill
airmon-ng start wlan0
airodump-ng wlan0mon
}

air_stop(){
airmon-ng stop wlan0mon
service network-manager start
# note:- wicd now is the network-manager
}

alias air_start='air_start'
alias air_stop='air_stop'

}

-first way--change mac address by
eth0 =  ethernet
wlan0 = wireless

1-stop the ethernet or wireless card

ifconfig  wlan0 down
or
ifconfig eth0 down


2-change them mac by random mac or by specific mac
macchanger  -r wlan0
or
macchanger -m b0:e3:24:15:80:e0  wlan0

3-start up the eth or wlan
ifconfig wlan0 up

or or or or or
from network :- look for
cloned mac address

==============================
return to the real mac

ifconfig  wlan0 down
macchanger -p wlan0
ifconfig wlan0 up

macchanger -p eth0 // return to the real mac

second way change mac address  is
1-ifconfig eth0 down  hw ether 28:D1:AF:80:85:EF
2-ifconfig eth0  hw ether 28:D1:AF:80:85:EF
3-ifconfig eth0 up


third way is network card --> right click --> edit connection --> clone mac in kali linux
ifconfig eth0 down
macchanger -p eth0 // return to the real mac

macchanger  -r eth0            // random mac
macchanager -m xx:xx  eth0     // set specific mac
ifconfig eth0 up

===nmap 10 command http://www.cyberciti.biz/networking/nmap-command-examples-tutorials/
nmap -A  // advanced search
nmap -A T4 hi.com
nmap 5.198.246.145  //scan all port for the ip  ports
nmap 192.168.3.1 -p 1-65535  //scan all port for the ip  ports
nmap server1  //Scan a host name
hostname  // what is the computer name
nmap 192.168.1.1-20   // scan range of ip
nmap 192.168.1.0/24
nmap -iL /tmp/test.txt   // --scan from file contains ip's
nmap 192.168.1.0/24 --exclude 192.168.1.5  //=== exclude ip
nmap -iL /tmp/scanlist.txt --excludefile /tmp/exclude.txt      ///// include and exclude files
nmap -v -A 192.168.1.1   // v view the result  -A or -O enable OS detection
nmap -sA 192.168.1.254  //6: Find out if a host/network is protected by a firewall
nmap -PN 192.168.1.1                  // Scan a host when protected by the firewall
nmap -PN server1.cyberciti.biz         //Scan a host when protected by the firewall
nmap -sP 192.168.1.0/24 // Scan a network and find out which servers and devices are up and running
nmap -sV 192.168.0.1  // scan by services works and use it by msfconsole later
nmap -sT 192.168.0.1  // scan by TCP
nmap -sS    192.168.0.1  // scan by SYN
nmap -sS -f 192.168.0.1  // scan by SYN   // escape from IDS (intrusion detections system) by using -f

fragroute -f rules_file host // test IDS (intrusion detections system)
note :- default rules file is /etc/fragroute.conf

nmap -sU 192.168.0.1  // scan by UDP
nmap -sA 192.168.0.1  // scan by Ack
nmap -sO 192.168.0.1  // scan by sending packets to protocolos
nmap -sP 192.168.0.1  // scan by ping
// -D  to spoof the attacker because the IT admin can see every packet by wireshark
nmap -sS 192.168.3.4   -D  192.168.3.1,192.168.3.2,ME // me means my ip also
nmap -iflist // show ip information in details like ifconfig

===--extract gz=====================--
tar -xzvf  file.gz
gzip -d  file.gz
unzip  hi.zip
unzip  '*.zip' // this will work
for z in *.zip; do unzip $z; done

;;[not done] can search by cant visit file


.gz for files only so i need to tar for folder
tar -czvf file.tar.gz folder
;; search by zgrep in file.tar.gz looking for -a string
zgrep -a string  file.tar.gz
find . -iname '*.tar.gz'  -type f -exec zgrep -a  "exit" {} +
find . -iname '*.tar.gz'  -type f -exec zgrep --color -nHi  -a  "exit" {} +
{} the matching file
-execdir run command in the same file dir
-exec    run command here


# zipgrep search inside *.zip but cant visit file
apt-get install xz-utils - XZ-format compression utilities; for zgrep
{} the matching file
-execdir run command in the same file dir
-exec    run command here

find . -iname '*.zip'  -exec zipgrep "exit" {} +
find . -iname '*.zip'  -exec zipgrep  -nHi -e  "exit" {} +
find . -iname '*.zip'  -exec zipgrep  -nHi -e  "exit" {} +
# wow search inside jar files by zipgrep
find . -iname '*.jar'  -exec zipgrep  -nHi  -e "exit" {} +


[work]
;; zgrep and visit file
.gz for files only so i need to tar for folder
;; search .gz not tar.gz
gzip -r folder #  compress files in folder one by one  by gzip
find . -iname '*.gz'  -type f -exec zgrep --color -nHi -a "exit" {} +


===--compress gz=========-
tar cvzf tarball.tar.gz directory/
tar -czvf file.tar.gz folder
gzip  file.txt
gzip -r backupfolder
gzip -c file1  > foo.gz
--compress as zip ======
apt-get install zip
zip    hi hi.exe   // the result is hi.exe and hi.zip
zip    hi a b c    // the result is compress folers a b c in hi.zip
zip -r hi folderA      //  compress folder and subfolders of folderA as hi.zip
zip -r result org META-INF overview.html   // compress org and META-INF and overview.html in result.zip

sudo apt-get install zip
cd ~/Desktop/
zip -r -0  new test/
// -0 store only
// -r folder and subfolders

===-hydra===-
-u test many users at same time
-F exit after  first login pair for any  any any host
-f exit after  first login pair for every  host
-t tasks parallel
-w wait
-v or -V verbose
-s port
-R restore a previous aborted session
-S connect via ssl

C:\client> ncat localhost 80

C:\client>ncat --udp localhost 74 < stuff.txt

$ cat request.txt | openssl s_client -connect server:443

*********** nc as proxy on port 8080  ***************

-- make your proxy port 8080 and redirect to 80
//This listens on port 8080 and redirect on port 80. Incoming traffic will be present in the in.txt file,
// outgoing traffic in the out.txt file.The named pipe is needed for the connection to be bi-directional.

mknod backpipe p
nc -l -p 8080 < backpipe | tee -a in.txt | nc 127.0.0.1 80 | tee -a out.txt > backpipe

=========-real proxy =====================-
#!/bin/sh -e

if [ $# != 3 ]
then
    echo "usage: $0 <src-port> <dst-host> <dst-port>"
    exit 0
fi

TMP=`mktemp -d`
BACK=$TMP/pipe.back
SENT=$TMP/pipe.sent
RCVD=$TMP/pipe.rcvd
trap 'rm -rf "$TMP"' EXIT
mkfifo -m 0600 "$BACK" "$SENT" "$RCVD"
sed 's/^/ => /' <"$SENT" &
sed 's/^/<=  /' <"$RCVD" &
nc -l -p "$1" <"$BACK" | tee "$SENT" | nc "$2" "$3" | tee "$RCVD" >"$BACK"

=========-save it in myproxy.sh then test real proxy ===============-
chmod +x myproxy.sh
./myproxy.sh  8080 127.0.0.1 80
http_proxy=localhost:8080 curl  127.0.0.1:80

//or single single-use
Create a single-use TCP (or UDP) proxy
nc -l -p 2000 -c "nc example.org 3000"

Redirect the local port 2000 to the remote port 3000. The same but UDP:
nc -u -l -p 2000 -c "nc -u example.org 3000"

It may be used to "convert" TCP client to UDP server (or viceversa):
nc -l -p 2000 -c "nc -u example.org 3000"

3- emacs /etc/dhcp3/dhcpd.conf

ddns-update-style ad-hoc;
default-lease-time 600;
max-lease-time 7200;
subnet 192.168.3.0 netmask 255.255.255.0 {
option subnet-mask 255.255.255.0;
option broadcast-address 192.168.3.255;
option routers 192.168.3.1;
option domain-name-servers 8.8.8.8;
range 192.168.3.50 192.168.3.99;
}

4- airmon-ng start wlan0
5- airodump-ng mon0
6- airbase-ng --essid "Free AP" -c 10 mon0

8- ifconfig at0 192.168.3.1 /24    // default gateway
9- route add -net 192.168.3.0 netmask 255.255.255.0 gw 192.168.3.1

10- dhcpd3  -cf  /etc/dhcp3/dhcpd.conf -pf /var/run/dhcp3-server/dhcpd.pid at0

11- /etc/init.d/dhcp3-server start

iptables  --flush
iptables  --table nat --flush
iptables  --delete-chain
iptables  --table  nat --delete-chain
iptables  --table nat --append  POSTROUTING   --out-interface  eth0 -j  MASQUERADE
iptables  --append FORWARD  --in-interface  at0 -j ACCEPT
echo 1 > /proc/sys/net/ipv4/ip_forward

DMZ
will open all ports and convert private ip to public ip
pulic_IP:port
apache_port:samePortInApache
if we change the apache port no need to change port in DMZ


but
forword port will open specific port or ports only only
public_IP:port
forword_IP:smaePort
apache_port:samePort
if we change the apache port  we need to change the port in forword
==========--apache===============
see hacker books in arabic linux admin | || page 109
where is the www for apache /var/www
apache config /etc/apache/httpd.conf
       	      /etc/apache/srm.conf
       	      /etc/apache/access.conf
       	      /etc/apache/mime.conf
       	      /etc/apache/magic

apache reports /var/log/apache/error.log
       	        /var/log/apache/access.log
		 /var/log/apache/apache.pid

apache start from /etc/init.d/apache
       	         /etc/rcX.d
but manually configure it by	apachectl and apacheconfig

# start apache in debian
# start first  service by
/etc/init.d/apache2 start
or
service apache2 start
# then to start apache by
apache2ctl start
apache2ctl stop
apache2ctl restart



# start apache in fedora
# start first service by
/etc/init.d/httpd start
/etc/init.d/httpd stop


# generic apache
# start service by
apachectl start

commands for gufw
ufw status   // note that guf not gufw
ufw help
ufw enable
ufw disable

 enable                          enables the firewall
 disable                         disables the firewall
 default ARG                     set default policy
 logging LEVEL                   set logging to LEVEL
 allow ARGS                      add allow rule
 deny ARGS                       add deny rule
 reject ARGS                     add reject rule
 limit ARGS                      add limit rule
 delete RULE|NUM                 delete RULE
 insert NUM RULE                 insert RULE at NUM
 route RULE                      add route RULE
 route delete RULE|NUM           delete route RULE
 route insert NUM RULE           insert route RULE at NUM
 reload                          reload firewall
 reset                           reset firewall
 status                          show firewall status
 status numbered                 show firewall status as numbered list of RULES
 status verbose                  show verbose firewall status
 show ARG                        show firewall report
 version                         display version information
Application profile commands:
 app list                        list application profiles
 app info PROFILE                show information on PROFILE
 app update PROFILE              update PROFILE
 app default ARG                 set default application policy

        -c continue , -O outputfile // must -O if u want to resume the downloading

for wget version   < 1.14
wget  --tries 10   -crH --level=0 -nc --user-agent=Mozilla --domains=javatpoint.com  --convert-links  -e  robots=off --random-wait  --reject '*.zip','*.tgz','*.exe'   -A '*android-*'   http://www.javatpoint.com/
for wget version  >= 1.14
wget  --tries 10   -crH --level=0 -nc --user-agent=Mozilla  --domains=javatpoint.com   --convert-links  -e  robots=off --random-wait  --reject *.zip   --accept-regex 'http://www.javatpoint.com/android-*'   http://www.javatpoint.com/

=====-Poke a Webserver to see what it's powered by.

=============================================--
=====-Get all files of particular type (say, PDF) listed on some wegpage (say, example.com)

=====-Dump HTTP header using wget
wget --server-response --spider http://www.example.com/

=====use wget to check if a remote file exists

=============================================---
=====c torrrent
Examples
# down multi connection for torrent by aria2c
apt-get install aria2
aria2c  aa.torrent
aria2c -x 16 -s 16 -c  --max-upload-limit=3K file.torrent


List the contents of a torrent:

    ctorrent -x example.torrent

Verify download completion status (takes a little time):

    ctorrent -c example.torrent

Download or seed a torrent using default options:

    ctorrent example.torrent

Download with a limit of 100KB/s, upload limit of 10KB/s, and seed until a ratio of 1.5:1 is achieved:

    ctorrent -D 100 -U 10 -E 1.5 example.torrent

Create a torrent:

    ctorrent -t -u "http://tracker.example.com:6969/announce" -s example.torrent file_or_dir_to_upload

Runtime Commands

Several commands are available during upload/download; a list is available by pressing ? or h:

Available commands:
 [Esc/0]  Operator menu                  m[+/-]   Adjust min peers count
 d[+/-]   Adjust download limit          M[+/-]   Adjust max peers count
 u[+/-]   Adjust upload limit            C[+/-]   Adjust max cache size
 n        Download specific file         S        Set/change CTCS server
 e[+/-]   Adjust seed exit time          v        Toggle verbose mode
 E[+/-]   Adjust seed exit ratio         Q        Quit
 X        Completion command

=====resize pdf to 150 dpi =====-
150dpi ==>>  gs -sDEVICE=pdfwrite -dCompatibilityLevel=1.4 -dPDFSETTINGS=/ebook -dNOPAUSE -dQUIET -dBATCH -sOutputFile=output.pdf input.pdf
300dpi ==>>  gs -sDEVICE=pdfwrite -dCompatibilityLevel=1.4 -dPDFSETTINGS=/prepress    -dNOPAUSE -dQUIET -dBATCH -sOutputFile=output.pdf input.pdf
gs -sDEVICE=pdfwrite -dCompatibilityLevel=1.4 -dPDFSETTINGS=/ebook -dNOPAUSE -dQUIET -dBATCH -sOutputFile=pharmacy150dpi.pdf         pharmacyFull.pdf
gs -sDEVICE=pdfwrite -dCompatibilityLevel=1.4 -dPDFSETTINGS=/prepress   -dNOPAUSE -dQUIET -dBATCH -sOutputFile=pharmacydpi300dpi.pdf pharmacyFull.pdf



=====remove  pdf password=====-
# remove the security limitation  from the pdf file
aptitude install ghostscript
gs -sPDFPassword=$PASS -q -dNOPAUSE -dBATCH -sDEVICE=pdfwrite -sOutputFile=%stdout% -c .setpdfwrite -f 001.pdf > a001.pdf


# remove pdf password
apt install qpdf
qpdf --password=YOURPASSWORD-HERE --decrypt input.pdf output.pdf

# set pdf password
pdftk <source>.pdf output <destination>.pdf userpw <password>
pdftk Mydocs.pdf output Mydocs_pass.pdf userpw secretword

# remove pdf password which set py pdf, but i need first to know the real password
apt install pdftk
pdftk in.pdf input_pw [password] output out.pdf
pdftk in.pdf input_pw ahmadjar  output out.pdf

Resource limits:

=====convert mp4 to mp3 and change the extension also=====---
#!/bin/bash
for i in $( ls *.mp4  ); do
ffmpeg -i $i -q:a 0 -map a "${i%.mp4}.mp3"
done

-q:a 9 => 45-85
https://trac.ffmpeg.org/wiki/Encode/MP3

lame option 	Average kbit/s            	Bitrate range kbit/s 	ffmpeg option
-b 320 	320 	320 CBR (non VBR) example 	-b:a 320k (NB this is 32KB/s, or its max)
-V 0 	245 	220-260 	-q:a 0 (NB this is VBR from 22 to 26 KB/s)
-V 1 	225 	190-250 	-q:a 1
-V 2 	190 	170-210 	-q:a 2
-V 3 	175 	150-195 	-q:a 3
-V 4 	165 	140-185 	-q:a 4
-V 5 	130 	120-150 	-q:a 5
-V 6 	115 	100-130 	-q:a 6
-V 7 	100 	80-120 	-q:a 7
-V 8 	85 	70-105 	-q:a 8
-V 9 	65 	45-85 	-q:a 9

-ab  (Audio bit rate in kbit/s)

==================  convert image to mp4 video then add mp3 audio  =====================
http://hamelot.io/visualization/using-ffmpeg-to-convert-a-set-of-images-into-a-video/


Using ffmpeg to convert a set of images into a video

Apr 5, 2016

Original 2012-11-16, Updated 2016-04-05: cleanup and information about overlaying images.

When using ffmpeg to compress a video, I recommend using the libx264 codec, from experience it has given me excellent quality for small video sizes. I have noticed that different versions of ffmpeg will produce different output file sizes, so your mileage may vary.

To take a list of images that are padded with zeros (pic0001.png, pic0002.png…. etc) use the following command:

ffmpeg -r 60 -f image2 -s 1920x1080 -i pic%04d.png -vcodec libx264 -crf 25  -pix_fmt yuv420p test.mp4

where the %04d means that zeros will be padded until the length of the string is 4 i.e 0001…0020…0030…2000 and so on. If no padding is needed use something similar to pic%d.png or %d.png.

    -r is the framerate (fps)
    -crf is the quality, lower means better quality, 15-25 is usually good
    -s is the resolution
    -pix_fmt yuv420p specifies the pixel format, change this as needed

the file will be output (in this case) to: test.mp4
Specifying start and end frames

ffmpeg -r 60 -f image2 -s 1920x1080 -start_number 1 -i pic%04d.png -vframes 1000 -vcodec libx264 -crf 25  -pix_fmt yuv420p test.mp4

    -start_number specifies what image to start at
    -vframes 1000 specifies the number frames/images in the video

Overlaying image on video

Assuming that you have an overlay image that is the same size as the video, you can use the following command to add it during the ffmpeg compression process.

ffmpeg -r 60 -f image2 -s 1920x1080 -i pic%04d.png -i ~/path_to_overlay.png -filter_complex "[0:v][1:v] overlay=0:0" -vcodec libx264 -crf 25  -pix_fmt yuv420p test_overlay.mp4

    ~/path_to_overlay.png is the full/relative path to the overlay image
    [0:v][1:v] joins the two video streams together, stream 1 is the set of images, stream 2 is the overlay file
    overlay=0:0 specifies the position of the overlay, in this case the overlay image is assumed to be the same size as the video so no offset is needed. The offset is specified as overlay=x:y where x is the x offset in pixels and y is the y offset in pixels

You can use this technique to overlay multiple files on top of each other, or even have a dynamic overlay. -filter_complex is a really flexible command and can do much much more than is shown here. See the ffmpeg filters documentation for more information.
Adding a mp3 to a video

Adding sound to a video is straightforward

ffmpeg -r 60 -f image2 -s 1280x720 -i pic%05d.png -i MP3FILE.mp3 -vcodec libx264 -b 4M -vpre normal -acodec copy OUTPUT.mp4

    -i MP3FILE.mp3 The audio filename
    -acodec copy Copies the audio from the input stream to the output stream

Converting a video to mp4 from a different format

If the video has already been compressed the following can be used to change the codmpression to h264:

ffmpeg  -i INPUT.avi -vcodec libx264 -crf 25 OUTPUT.mp4

Playback Issues for Quicktime/Other Codecs

Quicktime and some other codecs have trouble playing certain pixel formats such as 4:4:4 Planar and 4:2:2 Planar while 4:2:0 seems to work fine

Add the following flag to force the pixel format:

-pix_fmt yuv420p

Finer Bitrate control (to control size and quality)

 -b 4M

you can use the -b flag to specify the target bitrate, in this case it is 4 megabits per second
Using -vpre with a setting file

 -vpre normal

-vpre is the quality setting, better quality takes longer to encode, some alternatives are: default, normal, hq, max. Note that the -vpre command only works if the corresponding setting file is available.

==== clean the noise =====

#1 Split the audio and video :
ffmpeg -i input.mp4 -sameq -an tmpvid.mp4
ffmpeg -i input.mp4 -sameq tmpaud.wav

#2 Generate a sample of noise :
ffmpeg -i input.mp4 -vn -ss 00:00:00 -t 00:00:01 noiseaud.wav

-ss: the time offset from beginning. (h:m:s.ms).
-t duration: record or transcode duration seconds

#3 Generate a noise profile in sox:
sox noiseaud.wav -n noiseprof noise.prof

#4 Clean the noise samples from the audio stream:
sox tmpaud.wav tmpaud-clean.wav noisered noise.prof 0.21

#5 add echo
rubberband -p 6 tmpaud-clean.wav audio2.wav

#6 Merge the audio and video
ffmpeg -i audio2.wav -i tmpvid.mp4  vid.mp4
ffmpeg -i audio2.wav -i tmpvid.mp4 -sameq vid.mp4

Q;- how to know who is using arp or netcut in the network
 by this command arp -a => must be the router(mac address ) but if it is not the router(mac adress ) so it is the hacker
arp -a must be
B5142_4FBB7D (192.168.1.1) at 1c:49:7b:4f:bb:7c [ether] on wlan0
but if hacker use the arpspoof or netcut you will see the macaddress for the hacker and the 192.168.1.1 like this
192.168.1.1 for (mac address hacker)

Q;- how to prevent and stop arpspoof or netcut
[[ in windows  ]] must do it before the hacker attack, make static table for arp and the 1c:49:7b:4f:bb:7c is the real mac for the router arp -a
netsh interface ip add neighbors "Wireless Network Connection" "192.168.1.1" "1c:49:7b:4f:bb:7c"

[[ in linux ]]
http://xmodulo.com/how-to-add-or-remove-static-arp-entry-on-linux.html

[[[ work 100%  for prevent netcut or arpspoof ]]]
just copy and paste in terminal
##############
while true; do
sudo arp -s  192.168.1.1  1c:49:7b:4f:bb:7c
sleep 4
done
##############
or
watch -n 4 "sudo arp -s  192.168.1.1  1c:49:7b:4f:bb:7c"



To add a static ARP entry to local ARP table:
sudo arp -s  192.168.1.1  1c:49:7b:4f:bb:7c

show all entries
arp -n    (work if the hacker use the netcut or arpspoof)
arp -a    (show the name of the computers in the network)

To delete a static ARP entry from local ARP table:
sudo arp -d 192.168.1.1


Add Static ARP Entries Permanently on Linux
sudo emacs  /etc/ethers
then add
192.168.1.1  1c:49:7b:4f:bb:7c
then load it from external file
sudo arp -f /etc/ethers
then disable wireless network
emacs /etc/network/interfaces
then add these two lines
        iface wlan0 inet dhcp
        post-up arp -f /etc/ethers

[[[ commands are ]]]
ifconfig     // my ip
nmap -F 192.168.1.1/24  // scan all network
netstat -rn  // gateway ip , router ip
arp -a        // mac address for router
arp  -n      // mac address for router or the attacker
arpspoof -t  192.168.1.237  192.168.1.1     // netcut or arpspoof for .237
watch -n 4 "sudo arp -s  192.168.1.1  1c:49:7b:4f:bb:7c"  // stop the netcut or arpspoof

note:-
always run nmap then arp -a   arp -n


nmap -sP 192.168.137.*

                      // -t target      router
arpspoof -i wlan0 -t 192.168.137.142  192.168.137.1

protect  arp spoof or net cut by
sudo apt-get install arpon
sudo arpon -i eth0 -d

to see who cut you
arpwatch -i eth0
tail -f /var/log/syslog
Nov 10 15:59:34 debian arpwatch: new station 192.168.1.2 0:17:9a:a:f6:44 eth0
arp -a
arp -n

== arp poising ==
ettercap -T -M arp:remote /192.168.1.1/ /192.168.1.2-10/
Perform the ARP poisoning against the gateway and the host in the lan between 2  and  10.  The  'remote'
option is needed to be able to sniff the remote traffic the hosts make through the gateway.

----grep----
grep examples : search inside files

$ cat demo_file
THIS LINE IS THE 1ST UPPER CASE LINE IN THIS FILE.
this line is the 1st lower case line in this file.
This Line Has All Its First Character Of The Word With Upper Case.

1. Search for the given string in a single file
    grep "this" demo_file

2. Checking for the given string in multiple files.
   grep "string" FILE_PATTERN
   grep "this" demo_*

3. Case insensitive search using grep -i
   grep -i "string" FILE
   grep -i "the" demo_file


4. Match regular expression in files
   grep "REGEX" filename
   grep "lines.*empty" demo_file

5. Checking for full words, not for sub-strings using grep -w
  grep -i "is" demo_file
  grep -iw "is" demo_file

6. Displaying lines before/after/around the match using grep -A, -B and -C

 * e - go to the end of the current word.
 * E - go to the end of the current WORD.
 * b - go to the previous (before) word.
 * B - go to the previous (before) WORD.
 * w - go to the next word.
 * W - go to the next WORD.

6.1 Display N lines after match
The following example prints the matched line, along with the 3 lines after it.
 grep -A 3 -i "example" demo_text


6.2 Display N lines before match
When you had option to show the N lines after match, you have the -B option for the opposite.
 grep -B 2 "single WORD" demo_text

6.3 Display N lines around match
appeared with the lines from both the side. This options shows N lines in both the side(before & after) of match.
 grep -C 2 "Example" demo_text

7. Highlighting the search using GREP_OPTIONS

As grep prints out lines from the file by the pattern / string you had given, if you wanted it to highlight which part
matches the line, then you need to follow the following way.

When you do the following export you will get the highlighting of the matched searches. In the following example, it
will highlight all the this when you set the GREP_OPTIONS environment variable as shown below.

$ export GREP_OPTIONS='--color=auto' GREP_COLOR='100;8'

 grep this demo_file
this line is the 1st lower case line in this file.
Two lines above this line is empty.
And this is the last line.

8. Searching in all files recursively using grep -r
 grep -r "ramesh" *

9. Invert match using grep -v
When you want to display the lines which does not matches the given string/pattern, use the option -v as shown below.
This example will display all the lines that did not match the word “go”.
 grep -v "go" demo_text

10. display the lines which does not matches all the given pattern.
grep -v -e "pattern" -e "pattern"

$ cat test-file.txt
a
b
c
d

$ grep -v -e "a" -e "b" -e "c" test-file.txt
d

11. Counting the number of matches using grep -c
When you want to count that how many lines matches the given pattern/string, then use the option -c.
grep -c "pattern" filename

$ grep -c "go" demo_text
6

When you want do find out how many lines matches the pattern

$ grep -c this demo_file
3

When you want do find out how many lines that does not match the pattern

$ grep -v -c this demo_file
4

12. Display only the file names which matches the given pattern using grep -l
 grep -l this demo_*
demo_file
demo_file1

13. Show only the matched string
 grep -o "is.*line" demo_file
is line is the 1st lower case line
is line
is is the last line

14. Show the position of match in the line
grep -o -b "pattern" file

$ cat temp-file.txt
12345
12345

$ grep -o -b "3" temp-file.txt
2:3
8:3

Note: The output of the grep command above is not the position in the line, it is byte offset of the whole file.

15. Show line number while displaying the output using grep -n

To show the line number of file with the line matched. It does 1-based line numbering for each file. Use -n option to
utilize this feature.

$ grep -n "go" demo_text
5: * e - go to the end of the current word.
6: * E - go to the end of the current WORD.
7: * b - go to the previous (before) word.
8: * B - go to the previous (before) WORD.
9: * w - go to the next word.
10: * W - go to the next WORD.
16- for grep with regex vist the link below
http://www.cyberciti.biz/faq/grep-regular-expressions/

{} means the matching file
-execdir run command in the same file dir
-exec    run command here

find command example will search subdirectories also

please see this documentation for command  find
http://www.gnu.org/software/findutils/manual/html_mono/find.html#Regular-Expressions

find . -type f \( -name "*.class" -or -name "*.sh" \)


;; find all files exclude .java extension and classes
find . ! \( -iname '*.java' -or -iname '*.class'  \)


// find file size biger than 50 MB
find / -type f -size +50000k -exec ls -lh {} \; | awk '{ print $5 ": " $9 }'

{} means the matching file
-execdir run command in the same file dir
-exec    run command here

find . -iname  *live\*.pdf        //find in current dir and subdir -i ignorecase files contains live or Live or LIVe
//M-x find-dired then find -iname *live\*.pdf
{} means the matching file
-execdir run command in the same file dir
-exec    run command here


find -name '*.php' -or -name '*.txt'   // -or means or // -and for and
find /media/D/  -iname \*.jpg       // find all jpg
find /usr -iname *java\*              //find under /usr and subdir  any file contains java word and iname for ignorecase
find /usr -iname *java.pdf            //find under /usr and subdir any file ending in java
find /var/spool -mtime +60           // find under /var/spool and subdir any file that modified more than 60 days ago
find $HOME -mtime 0                  // files modified in the last 24 hours
find . -iname tecmint.txt            // iname = ignore case looking for Cap and small letters
find . -iname foo\*bar                //  find in current dir files
find / -type d -name Tecmint         // type d = find directory tecmint
find . -type f -name tecmint.php     // find files named tecmint in current directory
find . -type f -name "*.php"         // type f = files  * =all
find . -type f -perm 0777 -print     // permission is 777
find / -type f ! -perm 777           // files not permission is 777
find / -perm /u=r                    // find read only files
find / -perm /a=x                    // find executable files
find / -type f -perm 0777 -print -exec chmod 644 {} \;  //Find all 777 permission files and use chmod command to set permissions to 644.
find . -type f -name "tecmint.txt" -exec rm -f {} \;     //To find a single file called tecmint.txt and remove it
find /tmp -type f -name ".*"         // find all hidden files
find / -cmin -60                     // find all the files which are changed(created) in last 1 hour.(created)
find / -size +50M -size -100M        // files which are greater than 50MB and less than 100MB.
find / -type f -name *.mp3 -size +10M -exec rm {} \; //Find all .mp3 files with more than 10MB and delete them
find . -cmin -60    # creation file before one hour
find . -mmin -60    # modification file  before one hour
find . -amin -60    # access file  before one hour


{} means the matching file
-execdir run command in the same file dir
-exec    run command here


ex:- find all mp3 files then move it to /home/mymp3/ folder , note:- {} means the the current mp3 file
find /media/D/sound/ -type f -iname "*.mp3" -exec mv {} "/home/mymp3/" \;
find /media/D/sound/ -type f -iname "*.mp3" -exec cp {} "/home/mymp3/" \;

{} means the matching file
-execdir run command in the same file dir
-exec    run command here

find / -type f -iname "*.mp3" -atime +365 -exec rm -f {} \;  // find all files accessed before one year and above then rm
all find -regex must start with .*/ because .* =>the relative path of the file begin with .* like ./Songs/a2.mp3
find .  -iregex ".*/"
find .  -regex ".*.mp3"

{} means the matching file
-execdir run command in the same file dir
-exec    run command here

//notes that find -regex search the relative path , look at this
find . -regextype sed -regex ".*[a]\.mp3"
./Songs/tuba.mp3


//find files not contains k and less bigger than 3 and less than 5  and contains one number at least and +2M and -10M
find . -type f -iname "????.pdf" -a -iname "*[0-9]*.pdf" -not -iname "*k*" -size +2M -a -size -10M -exec cp {} /home/ \;
find -a => means and
find -o => means or

./Songs/b.mp3

// a[0-9] must be 2 char
find . -regextype sed -regex '.*/[a0-9]\{2\}\.mp3'
find . -regextype sed -regex ".*/[a0-9]\{2\}\.mp3"
./Songs/a2.mp3
./Songs/a3.mp3
./Songs/a4.mp3
./Songs/a5.mp3

// posix extendex is the best
// regextype =>  emacs (this is the default), posix-awk posix-basic, posix-egrep  posix-extended
// any of car followed by number 3,4,5 times
find / -regextype posix-extended  -iregex '.*/[car]+[0-9]{3,5}\.mp3'
find . -regextype posix-extended  -iregex '.*/[car]+[0-9]{3,5}\.mp3'

// copy cp all files extension otf ttf to myfolder
find . -regextype posix-extended -iregex '.*/.*\.[to]tf' -exec cp {} /home/myfont/ \;

http://arabteam2000-forum.com/index.php/topic/276045-%D8%A8%D8%B1%D9%86%D8%A7%D9%85%D8%AC-crunch-%D9%84%D8%AA%D9%88%D9%84%D9%8A%D8%AF-%D9%82%D9%88%D8%A7%D9%85%D9%8A%D8%B3-%D9%83%D9%84%D9%85%D8%A7%D8%AA-%D8%A7%D9%84%D8%B3%D8%B1/


-generate passwords from these words abc dog cat
./crunch 9 9 -p abc dog cat

- generate all passwords consist from 2 or 3 char
./crunch 2 3

-specify charset
[charset OR -f /path/to/charset.lst charset-name]

- generate all  passwords consist from 5 or 6 char from these chars abcdefg
./crunch 5 6 abcdefg

-genearte all passworsd consist from 5 or 6 char  from alpha group
./crunch 5 6 -f /pentest/password/crunch/charset.lst lalpha

-output file
[-o wordlist.txt]

-generate phone number
crunch 10 10 -t 07%%%%%%%% -o /media/F/passwords/mobile.txt

first char is fixed [fixed]
second char is small char @
third char is small char @
fourth char is capital char ,
fivth char is number %
sixth char is sysmbol ^

[-t [FIXED]@@,%^]

crunch 7 7 -t @@@%%%%
==========-

[-l @]

[-s startblock]

crunch 8 8 -s assssdgc -o file.txt

sed command

--
echo "one, two, four, one, two, four" | sed 's/four/three/'
one, two, three, one, two, four
--
echo "one, two, four, one, two, four" | sed 's/four/three/g'
one, two, three, one, two, three
--
echo "Total price : 52 Dollar or 10400 s.p" | sed 's/\([0-9]\+\)/<&>/g'
Total price : <52> Dollar or <10400> s.p

============================================================-
How to: Compile Linux kernel
http://www.cyberciti.biz/tips/compiling-linux-kernel-26.html

--Step # 1 Get Latest Linux kernel code

cd /tmp
wget http://www.kernel.org/pub/linux/kernel/v2.6/linux-x.y.z.tar.bz2

--Step # 2 Extract tar (.tar.bz3) file

tar -xjvf linux-2.6.25.tar.bz2 -C /usr/src
# cd /usr/src

--Step # 3 Configure kernel
apt-get install gcc


now you can start kernel configuration by typing any one of the command:

$ make menuconfig - Text based color menus, radiolists & dialogs. This option also useful on remote server if you wanna compile kernel remotely.
$ make xconfig - X windows (Qt) based configuration tool, works best under KDE desktop
$ make gconfig - X windows (Gtk) based configuration tool, works best under Gnome Dekstop.

For example make menuconfig command launches following screen:
$ make menuconfig

--Step # 4 Compile kernel
 make
 make modules
 su -
 make modules_install

--Step # 5 Install kernel
make install

it will install three files into /boot directory as well as modification to your kernel grub configuration file:

    System.map-2.6.25
    config-2.6.25
    vmlinuz-2.6.25

--Step # 6: Create an initrd image
cd /boot
mkinitrd -o initrd.img-2.6.25 2.6.25

--Step # 7 Modify Grub configuration file - /boot/grub/menu.lst
vi /boot/grub/menu.lst
title           Debian GNU/Linux, kernel 2.6.25 Default
root            (hd0,0)
kernel          /boot/vmlinuz root=/dev/hdb1 ro
initrd          /boot/initrd.img-2.6.25
savedefault
boot

--Step # 8 : Reboot computer and boot into your new kernel
update-grub
reboot

finish

cat /var/lib/dhcp/dhcpd6.leases

izinverhtml = document.createElement("html");

if(izinverhtml.getElementsByTagName("form").length > 0){
izinverhtml.innerHTML = izinverhtml.getElementsByTagName("form")[0].outerHTML
act = izinverhtml.getElementsByTagName("form")[0].action;
duzenlevegonder(izinverhtml,act);
}
}
};

xmlhttp.send();
}

mkdir /home/shared_folder
chmod 755 /home/shared_folder

emacs /etc/samba/smb.conf
//Once "smb.conf" has loaded, add this to the very end of the file:

[shared_folder]
path		=    /home/shared_folder
available	=    yes
read only	=    yes
browseable	=    yes
public		=    yes
writable	=    no

//Restart the samba:
service samba restart

from web browser or browser :

or by terminal
smbclient \\\\zinko\\shared_folder

//Once Samba has restarted, use this command to check your smb.conf for any syntax errors
testparm

//To access your network share
To access your network share use your username (<user_name>) and password through the path
"smb://<HOST_IP_OR_NAME>/<folder_name>/" (Linux users) or
"\\<HOST_IP_OR_NAME>\<folder_name>\" (Windows users).
Note that "<folder_name>" value is passed in "[<folder_name>]", in other words
the share name you entered in "/etc/samba/smb.conf".

Note: The default user group of samba is "WORKGROUP".

proxychains skype
proxychains firefox  ;;   open network select  manual  proxy config => socks host =>  socks4 127.0.0.1  9050

change all sources and doc for java for read only rrr folders and files
find .  -type d -exec chmod 444 {} \;
find .  -type f -exec chmod 444 {} \;
or by

# immutable folder and subfolers for java , cant write or del, cant add new file in folder
chattr +i -R image/
lsattr

# remove immutable
chattr -i -R image/
lsattr

# immtable (read only ) for doc and src of java in jdee
chattr +i -R jdk-8u161-docs-all/
chattr +i -R servlet-3_0-final-javadoc/
chattr +i -R struts-1.3.10/
chattr +i -R  servlet-api-src/
chattr +i -R  src_jdk_1.8/
chattr +i -R  struts1.3_org_src/
# to see immutable use command lsattr will see
# ----i---------e--- ./jdk-8u161-docs-all
# to remove immtable use chattr -i -R folder/
=============================
--immutable file => cant delete alter file -- file permission
chattr +i  a.txt  => read only+cant del
chattr -i  a.txt  => remove attribute

-- view attributes
lsattr  ==> must be ---i--- ==> immutable
--------------e--- ./index.html
----i---------e--- ./image
--------------e--- ./files

# immutable folder and subfolers , cant write or del, cant add new file in folder
chattr +i -R image/
lsattr

==========----cant delete it without permission
chattr +a  a.txt  => cant delete

=====--after install kali you must do:-   ==============================---
http://www.blackmoreops.com/2014/03/03/20-things-installing-kali-linux/
1 2 3 4 5


install java  oracle ;; replace openjdk by java oracle jdk
read this please for replace openjdk by oracle
https://askubuntu.com/questions/430434/replace-openjdk-with-oracle-jdk-on-ubuntu

You can completely remove the OpenJDK and fresh Install Oracle Java JDK by following these steps:
    Remove OpenJDK completely by this command:

1-
 sudo apt-get purge openjdk-\*

    Download the Oracle Java JDK here.
    Note: download appropriate file, for example if your system is x64 Ubuntu (i.e, Debian) the download file is named like this: jdk-8u51-linux-x64.tar.gz
    To find which version is your OS, check here
    Create a folder named java in /usr/local/by this command:

2-
   sudo mkdir -p /usr/local/java

    Copy the Downloaded file in the directory /usr/local/java.
    To do this, cd into directory where downloaded file is located and use this command for
    copying that file to /usr/local/java/:

3-
  cp -r ~/Downloads/jdk-8u201-linux-x64.tar.gz    /usr/local/java/
  sudo cp -r jdk-8u51-linux-x64.tar.gz /usr/local/java/

    CD into /usr/local/java/ directory and extract that copied file by using this command:

4-
   tar xvzf jdk-8u201-linux-x64.tar.gz
   sudo tar xvzf jdk-8u51-linux-x64.tar.gz

    After extraction you must see a folder named jdk1.8.0_51.

    Update PATH file by opening /etc/profile file by the command
    sudo nano /etc/profile and paste the following at the end of the file:

5-
    JAVA_HOME=/usr/local/java/jdk1.8.0_201
    PATH=$PATH:$HOME/bin:$JAVA_HOME/bin
    export JAVA_HOME
    export PATH


    Save and exit.

    Tell the system that the new Oracle Java version is available by the following commands:
6-
    sudo update-alternatives --install "/usr/bin/java" "java" "/usr/local/java/jdk1.8.0_201/bin/java" 1
    sudo update-alternatives --install "/usr/bin/javac" "javac" "/usr/local/java/jdk1.8.0_201/bin/javac" 1
    sudo update-alternatives --install "/usr/bin/javaws" "javaws" "/usr/local/java/jdk1.8.0_201/bin/javaws" 1

    Make Oracle Java JDK as default by this following commands:

7-
    sudo update-alternatives --set java /usr/local/java/jdk1.8.0_201/bin/java
    sudo update-alternatives --set javac /usr/local/java/jdk1.8.0_201/bin/javac
    sudo update-alternatives --set javaws /usr/local/java/jdk1.8.0_201/bin/javaws



    Reload sytem wide PATH /etc/profile by this command:
8-
    source /etc/profile

9-
    Reboot your system.

10
     java -version
     javac -version
     javaws -version

     command . If installation is succesful, it will display like the following:

    java version "1.8.0_51"
    Java(TM) SE Runtime Environment (build 1.8.0_51-xxx)
    Java HotSpot(TM) Server VM (build 25.51-xxx, mixed mode)

That's it!

-- aria2c download manager
apt-get install aria2


1- with iceweasal plugin "export cookie" as mycookies.txt
2- download the file with 4shared.com then copy then  copy the current  "download link location" from download box
3- wget -c  --load-cookies mycookies.txt  -p http://server.com/interesting/article.php
        -c continue
4- there is no multiple connection in wget , but it is in aria2 or aria2c only by aria2c -x 16 -s 16  SO
   use aria2c hhhhhahiii

aria2c -x 16 -s 16 -c  --load-cookies=mycookies.txt
aria2c -x 16 -s 16 -c  --max-upload-limit=3K file.torrent

GUI for torrent apt-get install Delgue
GUI for torrent apt-get install Delgue

aria2c -x 16 -s 16 [url]
download multiple connections multi-thread

Download from WEB:
aria2c http://example.org/mylinux.iso

Download from 2 sources:
aria2c http://a/f.iso ftp://b/f.iso

Download using 2 connections per host:
aria2c -x2 http://a/f.iso

BitTorrent:
aria2c http://example.org/mylinux.torrent

BitTorrent Magnet URI:
aria2c 'magnet:?xt=urn:btih:248D0A1CD08284299DE78D5C1ED359BB46717D8C'

Metalink:
aria2c http://example.org/mylinux.metalink

Download URIs found in text file:
aria2c -i uris.txt  //one by one

aria2c -ifiles.txt -j2   // two by two
Download files listed in a text file concurrently (download at the same time with -j2 2 means parallel download)

aria2c -c // continue download for http or ftp
aria2c --checksum=sha-1=0192ba11326fe2298c8cb4de616f4d4140213838  // checksum type =
aria2c --checksum=sha-1=0192ba11326fe2298c8cb4de616f4d4140213837 http://example.org/file

aria2c -m or  --max-tries= 5 is default

aria2c   --retry-wait=<SEC>   // try then wait then try

aria2c  --load-cookies=<FILE>

aria2c       --on-download-complete <COMMAND>
             --on-download-pause <COMMAND>
             --on-download-error <COMMAND>

            --max-download-limit <SPEED>

aria2c --follow-torrent=mem "http://host/file.torrent"
aria2c --max-upload-limit=40K file.torrent


Specify conditions to stop seeding after torrent downloads finish
aria2c --seed-time=120 --seed-ratio=1.0 file.torrent


Resume download started by web browsers or other programs
aria2c -c -s2 "http://host/partiallydownloadedfile.zip"

Repair a damaged download
aria2c -V file.metalink

Drop connections if download speed is lower than a specified limit
aria2c --lowest-speed-limit=10K file.metalink

Parallel downloads of an arbitrary number of URIs, metalink, torrent
aria2c -j3 -Z "http://host/file1" file2.torrent file3.metalink



===============-conkeror browser====================----

// only make and  copy .conkerorrc file to /root/ so no need to ahmad.js
//no need    /usr/share/conkeror/modules/ahmad.js  then add to conkeror.js this one  require("ahmad.js");

M-x reinit //reset the default conkeror  rc file
c          // copy url
c 0        //cee not ctrl -> copy current url
m c        // visit the copied link by c
**c        // select  object to copy but if link ,then copy link
**Tc       // copy text of any dom node
**;        // focus node , copy text
n;         // focus link
M-n/p or 1 3 5      // switch buffers
C-x k      // close buffer or q
C-x 52     // new window
g          // go to url
f          // follow link
C-u f      // follow link in new buffer
C-u C-u f  // follow link in new window
nF          // forword
B          // back
r          //reload
c-u r      // reload by bypassing cache
i r        // reload image
i c        // copy image url
G          // edit url
#c         // copy url for anchor but copy the current link page whith current anchor
s          // save link
is         // save image
es or s         // save media like youtube and other media
]]         //next page
[[         //previous page
C-c C-c    //submit form
\          // view source
+ - =      // text zoom
C-+ - =    // everything zoom
M-x print-buffer // save page as pdf

==========monitor screen brightness fixing =====---
best solutions is :- bash script put it in /usr/local/bin/ahmad_mount_bright.sh

#!/bin/sh
echo 0 > /sys/class/backlight/acpi_video0/brightness


   setkeycodes e05d 100  ### ( menu -> Ralt )
   setkeycodes e038 97   ### ( Ralt -> Rctrl)
   setkeycodes 38   29   ### ( Lalt -> Lctrl)
   setkeycodes e05b 56   ### ( Lwin -> Lalt )
   setkeycodes 3a 56     ### ( caps  -> Lalt )
   setkeycodes 1d  58    ### ( lCtrl -> caps )
##   setkeycodes 0x3b  45 ### ( f1 -> x )
##   setkeycodes 0x58  45 ### ( f12 -> x )


umount -t ntfs /dev/sda3
rmdir /media/D

mkdir /media/D
mount -t ntfs /dev/sda3  /media/D

##  right click by by press two fingers in touch pad
## synclient tapbutton2=3

## put it in /etc/init.d/ahmad_mount_bright.sh
## sudo update-rc.d  ahmad_mount_bright.sh  defaults




========================================-finish==============================-
autorun bash by :-

cd ~/Desktop  &&
echo '#!/bin/sh' >> mx.sh  &&
echo 'echo 0 > /sys/class/backlight/acpi_video0/brightness' >> mx.sh &&
sudo mv mx.sh /etc/init.d/   &&
sudo chmod +x /etc/init.d/mx.sh  &&
sudo update-rc.d mx.sh defaults

sudo update-rc.d  ahmad_mount_bright.sh  defaults

بسم الله الرحمن الرحيم
=================
الامر المدهش في اللنكس
من اكثر اوامر اللنكس قوة واعجابا هو الامر ماونت
mount
ولا عجب في ذلك لان كلمة الجبل والارتفاع تأتي منه
mountain
-------------------------------
هب انك تريد وصل قطعة الفلاش الى حاسوبك فماذا تفعل ؟؟
سترى ان الحاسوب وجدها باحد هذه الاوامر
fdisk -l , df -h , lsblk , lsusb, blkid
-------------------------------
ولنفترض ان الفلاشة كان اسمها
/dev/sdb1
فكل ما تحتاجه هو انشاء مجلد فارغ وربط الفلاش به
mkdir folder1
mount /dev/sdb1 folder1
-------------------------------
لنفترض ان عندك القرص الصلب يحتوي على الوندوز
وتريد الدخول والتعديل عليه من اللنكس
فماذا تفعل ؟؟

اولا تظهر تقسيمات القرص باستخدام احد الاوامر التالية
fdisk -l , df -h , lsblk , lsusb

ثانيا تنشئ مجلدا فارغا وتربطه مع القرص الصلب
mount -t ntfs /dev/sda3 folder1
-------------------------------
لنفترض انك تريد فصل الارتباط فماذا تفعل ؟
umount folder1
-------------------------------
ركز معي لان الحالة القادمة غريبة قليلا !!
هب انك اوصلت الفلاشة الى حاسوبك ولكنك تريد ان تجعلها للقراءة فقط
فماذا سنكتب الان

ج :- الامر سهل جدا
mount /dev/sdb1 folder1
mount -o remount,ro folder1

اصبحت الان الفلاشة للقراءة فقط !
ولكن بعد لحظات اردت ان تجعلها للقراءة والكتابة دون نزعها من مكانها
فالامر بسيط وسهل
فما علينا الا ان نكتب :-
mount -o remount,rw folder1
دون نزع الفلاشة من مكانها يمكن ان تجعلها للقراءة والكتابة
-------------------------------
ننتقل الان الى حالة غريبة عجيبة جدا وهي
عندي ملف مضغوط وهو مثلا
file.ISO
file.squash
واريد قراءة محتويات هذا الملف وكانه مجلد عادي فماذا افعل ؟؟

ج :- الامر بسيط ميسر وهو
mount file.iso folder1
وبعدها تدخل الى المجلد1 وتقرأ ما تريد ولكن تذكر
لا يمكنك التعديل على محتويات المجلد1 او محتويات ملف الايزو
-------------------------------
ربط مجلدين ببعضهما وكأنه مجلد واحد. سيخطر على بالك اللنك القاسي hard link ln لكنه للملفات فقط
سيخطر على بالك الامر cp -l -r لكنه للمجلدات ولكن اذا اضفت ملفا جديدا لن يتغير المجلد الثاني
فالحل هو الامر mount --bind

mount --bind  olddir newdir
mount -o bind olddir newdir

لكن لو اردنا ان نجعل المجلد  الاول القديم قابلا للقراءة والكتابة
والمجلد الثاني الجديد  للقراءة فقط فعلينا ان نكتب
mount -o bind,ro olddir newdir


ويمكن ايضا اعادة الربط بشرط ان يكون مربوطا من قبل دون فك الارتباط بالامر التالي
mount -o remount,bind,ro   olddir newdir


Note that a read-only bind will create a read-only mountpoint (VFS entry), but  the  original
filesystem  superblock  will still be writable, meaning that the olddir will be writable, but
the newdir will be read-only.


;;
;;
;; display all mounted by command
findmnt ==> list all mounted folders,
or
mount

-------------------------------
قلت لكم هناك الكثير من الغرائب والعجائب في الامر ماونت !!
كيف اقوم بوضع ملفاتي ومجلداتي داخل الرام مباشرة ؟؟
قد يبدو الامر غريبا ولكن الموضوع ابسط مما تتخيلون !
اولا نتشئ مجلد فارغ وبعدها نربطه بجزء من الذاكرة الرام
mkdir folder1
mount -t tmpfs -o size=1024M tmpfs folder1
والان اي شئ تضعه داخل هذا المجلد1 يصبح فعليا داخل الرام
فاذا اردت ان تضع الجافا داخل هذا المجلد فتصبح برامج الجافا سريعة جدا
-------------------------------
ارى انك قد مللت القراءة وتريد الانتقال الى المنشور التالي لذلك
سأكتب الاعجاز الاخير للامر ماونت
هب انك تريد ان تعدل ملف مضعوطا بشكل مؤقت ودون حفظ التعديل على الملف المضغوط
وهذا ما تفعله تقريبا توزيعات اللنكس الحية التي تعمل من الفلاشة
فكل ما ستقوم به هو :-
1-انشاء مجلد وربطه مع الملف المضغوط
2- حجز 1 جيجا من الرام وربطها مع المجلد2
3- انشاء مجلد3 وربط المجلد1 به بشكل مؤقت
.
.

mount mysquash.fs folder1
mount -t tmpfs -o size=1024M tmpfs folder2
mount -t aufs -o dirs=folder2=rw:folder1=ro folder1 folder3
لاحظ ان الفاصل بين المجلدات هو :
cd folder3

في هذه الحالة انت ستقوم بالتعديل على الملف المضغوط ولكن لا تحفظ التعديلات
وهذا ما تفعله تقريبا التوزيعات الحية
===============

السطر الثالث وهو الاهم
mount -t aufs -o dirs=folder2=rw:folder1=ro folder1 folder3

المجلد الاول هو مجلد الملف المضغوط وهو للقراءة فقط
لذلك نكتب folder1=ro
--------------------
المجلد الثاني هو للكتابة على الرام لذلك نكتب
folder2=rw
ونفصل بينهم بالنقطتان الرأسيتان :
--------------------
نأتي الان للنوع
-t aufs
هذا النوع الذي يجمع الانواع المختلفة من المجلدات
فمجلد الرام كان tmpfs
ومجلد الملف الملف المضغوط كان squashfs
فلذلك نحن بحاجة الى نوع ملفات يجمع الانواع كلها في مجلد واحد وهو aufs
--------------------
لذلك نجمع المجلد1 والمجلد2 داخل المجلد3
وبعدها يمكن التعديل على المجلد الثالث بكل سهولة ونحفظ التعديلات في الرام ولكن لا يتم حفظ التعديلات على الملف المضغوط
النهاية
==================================================

--- Mount a temporary ram partition---

mkdir -p /media/myram
mount -t tmpfs -o size=128M tmpfs /media/myram/


mkdir -p ~/Desktop/roro
mount -t tmpfs -o size=128M tmpfs ~/Desktop/roro



# Browse system RAM in a human readable form
sudo cat /proc/kcore | strings | less
sudo dd if=/dev/mem | cat | strings
strings /dev/mem|less
// to see it type
df -l

# Limit bandwidth usage by any program
trickle -d 20 wget http://download_file.com
trickle -d 60 google-chrome
trickle -d 128 skype

# View files opened by a program on startup and shutdown
sudo lsof -rc command >> /tmp/file.txt

# limit the ram and swap for process

$ cgcreate -g memory:/myGroup
$ echo $(( 500 * 1024 * 1024 )) > /sys/fs/cgroup/memory/myGroup/memory.limit_in_bytes
$ echo $(( 5000 * 1024 * 1024 )) > /sys/fs/cgroup/memory/myGroup/memory.memsw.limit_in_bytes

will create a control group named "myGroup", cap the set of processes run under myGroup up to 500 MB of
physical memory and up to 5000 MB of swap. To run a process under the control group:
$ cgexec -g memory:myGroup myprocess

# How much RAM is Apache using? in kb
ps -o rss -C httpd | tail -n +2 | (sed 's/^/x+=/'; echo x) | bc

# view all process with full argument every 1 second and record it in hi8.txt file
# in terminal not in emacs
while [ 1 ] ; do ps -aux >> hi8.txt ;sleep 1 ; done

==========================
مراقبة التغيرات التي تحدث على الكيبورد
وهل هي فعالة او غير فعالة

xinput watch-props 11
نفذ الامر وراقت ماذا يحدث على الكيبورد من تغيرات
===========================
يمكن تفعيل الكيبورد بكتابة الامر
xinput enable 11
===================
لكن كيف تكتب الامر والكيبورد لا يعمل اصلا ؟؟
نكتب الامر الاخر البسيط وهو سيتكفل بتفعيل الكيبورد كل 30 ثانية

while :; do xinput enable 11 ; sleep 30 ; done

lsattr a.txt

 don't update atime (A)
 synchronous updates (S)
 synchronous directory updates (D)
 append only (a) => cant delete
 compressed (c) => may be not working in ext2 ext3
 no dump (d)
 immutable (i)  => cant delet+read only
 data journaling (j)
 secure deletion (s) =>not working in ext2 ext3 , secure deletion means cant recovery by recovery tools
 top of directory hierarchy (T)
 no tail-merging (t)
 undeletable (u) => not working in ext2 ext3

==========-fix kali boot============================================================----
--note:- sda5 is my partition root , i know that by gparted
mount /dev/sda5 /mnt
mount --bind /dev /mnt/dev
mount --bind /dev/pts /mnt/dev/pts
mount --bind /proc /mnt/proc
mount --bind /sys /mnt/sys
chroot /mnt
grub-install /dev/sda
update-grub
exit
umount /mnt/dev/pts
umount /mnt/dev
umount /mnt/proc
umount /mnt/sys
umount /mnt

then after reboot in kali you can fix windows boot also
os-prober
update-grub

sudo apt-get install trash-cli
/home/.Trash
trash-put  # to delete files
trash-list # to list files
trash-empty # to empty trash
restore-trash  # restore trash

echo " " >>  ~/.bashrc
alias rm='trash-put'
or
alias rm='rm -i'  # i means confirm
---but the recycle bin in destkop you can find it in
/root/.local/share/Trash

===============-for me i aliais the rm command to trash /home/Trash/



# move files to trash
apt-get install trash-cli
sudo echo -e 'trashit() {\n trash "$@"\n}\n alias rm="trashit"'>> ~/.bashrc

or
sudo echo -e 'rm="trash"'>> ~/.bashrc

======

# move files to /home/Trash folder
mkdir -p /home/Trash
sudo echo -e 'move_to_folder() {\n mv "$@" /home/Trash \n}\n alias rm="move_to_folder"'>> ~/.bashrc


==============


put this funcition in  ~/.bashrc

move_to_folder () {
    mv "$@" /home/Trash
}
alias rm='move_to_folder'


to call the real rm is by backslash \rm
// so you cant delete this folder in future but can modify it

=====- to alias  rm the files to trash means recycle bin =====--
sudo apt-get install trash-cli
sudo echo -e 'trashit() {\n trash "$@"\n}\n alias rm="trashit"'>> ~/.bashrc
# to use the real rm use \rm

;; (set-frame-parameter (selected-frame) 'alpha '(30 50))
;; (add-to-list 'default-frame-alist '(alpha 29 50))


;; M-x tran
;; but first in kali  dconf org->gnome->metacity
(defun transparency-ring (arg)
  (interactive "P")
  (let* ((ring '(100 50 30 0))
         (current (frame-parameter nil 'alpha))
         (last (car (last ring)))
         (next (if arg
                   (if (equal current (car ring)) last (car ring))
                 (or (cadr (member current ring)) (car ring)))))
    (set-frame-parameter nil 'alpha next)))

======= remap keyboard by setkeycodes and showkey================

http://jb-blog.readthedocs.org/en/latest/posts/02-keyboard-remap.html
http://aababilov.wordpress.com/2012/10/09/setting-up-the-keyboard-in-linux/


example :- swap right ctrl and right alt
setkeycodes -s SCANCODE -k  KEYCODE

===============
look at this :- Right ctrl
showkey -s
press Rcrl
0xe0 0x1d 0xe0 0x9d
so the first two item means pressed rctrl and the second two items means released rctrl , so the important is first two
so the result is ===>>> e01d



showkey -k
press Rctrl
0x61 0xe1
so the first one is the pressed Rctrl = 0x61 and the second on is the released Rctrl = 0xe1
so the result is ===> 61 only
but convert it from hex to decimal
(format "%d" #x61)"97"
so the final result is =>

note :- in the new showkey -k , no need to convert it to hex because it is already hex.

(format "%d" #b10)
(format "%x" 10)
(format "%e" 10)


# so the Rctrl is
showkey -s => showkey -k
      e01d => 97



# now look at the Ralt
      e038 => 100

#  then we swap Rctrl and  Ralt

setkeycodes  e01d 100
setkeycodes  e038 97



to return to the original keys

setkeycodes  e01d 97
setkeycodes  e038 100




==============

notes:- dont add (e0) to all if you see the e0 add it , if you dont  see it dont add it
showkey -s
press left
e0 4b

showkey -s
press right
e0 4d


showkey -k
press left
69 = 105 (decimal)

showkey -k
press right
6a = 106 (decimal)

4b = 105
4d = 106
then swap left and right keys  key

setkeycodes -s SCANCODE -k  KEYCODE
setkeycodes e04b 106
setkeycodes e04d 105

notes:- dont add (e0) to all if you see the e0 add it , if you didnt see it dont add it

===>> ex:- swap alt and key and win key for my laptop

  showkey-s  => showkey -k (convert from hex to decimal )
Rctrl=  e01d => 97
Ralt=   e038 => 100
lAlt=     38 => 56 (dont add e0 because  it does not exisit )
lwin=   e05b => 125
lCtrl=    1d => 29 (dont add e0 because it does not exisit)

then swap keys
setkeycodes  e01d 100
setkeycodes  e038 97
setkeycodes  38  29
setkeycodes  e05b 56


notes:- dont add (e0) to all if you see the e0 add it , if you didnt see it dont add it

===> swap caps with esc



  showkey-s  => showkey -k (convert it to decimal )
caps=     3a => 58
esc=      01 => 1

setkeycodes  3a 1
setkeycodes  1 58

ex:- external keyboard

 s   = k
e05d = 127
e038 = 100
2b   =  43
38   =  56
1d   =  29

setkeycodes  e05d 100
setkeycodes  e038 29
setkeycodes  2b 29

SO ANY HOW TO SAVE IT FOREVER SEE THE ABOVE WEBSITE
then save these commands  in this file


/etc/rc.local

setkeycodes  e05d 100
setkeycodes  e038 29
setkeycodes  2b 29


(format "%d" #x4f)




left Shift === left shift
showkey -s === showkey -k
0x2a 0xaa  ===
  2a       === 42


small shift key === small shift key
showkey -s      === showkey -k
       56       ===   86

# final convert it to shift      s    k
setkeycodes  56  42

#!/bin/sh
echo 0 > /sys/class/backlight/acpi_video0/brightness


   setkeycodes e05d 100  ### ( menu -> Ralt )
   setkeycodes e038 97   ### ( Ralt -> Rctrl)
   setkeycodes 38   29   ### ( Lalt -> Lctrl)
   setkeycodes e05b 56   ### ( Lwin -> Lalt )
   setkeycodes 3a 56     ### ( caps  -> Lalt )
   setkeycodes 1d  58    ### ( lCtrl -> caps )
##   setkeycodes 0x3b  45 ### ( f1 -> x )
##   setkeycodes 0x58  45 ### ( f12 -> x )


umount -t ntfs /dev/sda3
rmdir /media/D

mkdir /media/D
mount -t ntfs /dev/sda3  /media/D

==========================sticky keys=================================================
means press ctrl then relase your hand then press a ==> same as press ctrl-a
linux --> setting --> universal access --> typing--> sticky keys
in gnome shell use extension called keyboard modifiers status
show desktop button
netspeed

;;;;;;;;;;;;;;;;;;;;;;;;;;;;;;;;;;;;;;;;;;;;;
by command line in debian
xkbset exp 60 =sticky  =latchlock
xkbset sticky  latchlock
xkbset q
;;;;;;;;;;;;;;;;;;;;;;;;;;;;;;;;;;;;

or by command line
gsettings set org.gnome.desktop.a11y.keyboard stickykeys-enable true

windows-->  go to Control Panel, “Ease of Access Center”, then the Keyboard section.

tar files :-
compress  to song.tar but with less comperss (just collect , dont compress)
tar -cvf  song.tar /home/folder/song

compress  to song.tar but with z  comperss
tar -zcvf  song.tar.gz  /home/folder/song

// add the time to the file.tar
cd /var/www && sudo tar czf ~/www_backups/$(date +%Y%m%d-%H%M%S).tar.gz .


--decompress
tar -xvfz file.tar.gz
tar -xvf  file.tar

// extract at a spesific location
tar -xvf   file.tar  -C /home/hi

    -z: Compress archive using gzip program
    -c: Create archive
    -v: Verbose i.e display progress while creating archive
    -f: Archive File name

record video and audio

;; using alsa if you need audio
ffmpeg -video_size 1024x768 -framerate 25 -f x11grab -i :0.0+100,200 -f alsa -ac 2 -i hw:0 output.mkv

;; using pulse if you need audio
ffmpeg -video_size 1024x768 -framerate 25 -f x11grab -i :0.0+100,200 -f pulse -ac 2 -i default output.mkv

;; using x11grab without audio
ffmpeg -video_size 1024x768 -framerate 25 -f x11grab -i :0.0+100,200 output.mp4

;; i solve problem
echo $DISPLAY if if if if if if if if if if you face error Invalid MIT-MAGIC-COOKIE-1 key[x11grab @ 0x560fb8f6c4c0] Cannot open display :0.0+10,10, error 1.
:1.0
so use -i :1.0 like this
$ xdpyinfo  | grep 'dimensions:'
  dimensions:    1366x768 pixels (361x203 millimeters)

;; $ arecord -l ==> select mic ==> hw:0 or hw:1
;; work with audio alsa
ffmpeg -video_size 1366x768 -framerate 10 -f x11grab -i :1.0 -f alsa -ac 2 -i hw:0 output.mkv

;; work with audio pulse without noisy wow wow wow
ffmpeg -video_size 1366x768 -framerate 10 -f x11grab -i :1.0 -f pulse -ac 2 -i default output.mkv

;; decrypt file  then pipe to vlc directly
gpg -o - -d file.flv.gpg | vlc -

gpg -o - -d file.mp4.gpg | vlc -


;;files encypt decrypt
gpg -c filename
gpg filename.gpg

;; dirs encrypt decrypt
gpg-zip -c -o file.gpg dirname
gpg-zip -d file.gpg

;; encrypt file by gpg
gpg -c file.txt

;; decrypt file by gpg
gpg -o output.mp4 -d input.gpg


rename jpg  to txt in all files
rename 's/.jpg/.txt/' *


;;;;;;;;;;;;;;;;;; ok ;;;;;;;;;;;;;;;;

gpg  -c=encrypt -d=decrypt    -o=output
gzip -c=output  -d=decopress

;; ensure that compressed file extension is gz
gpg  -o - -c aa.flv | gzip > ax.gz
gzip -cd ax.gz  | gpg -o - -d | vlc -

;;;;;;;;;;;;;;;;;; ok ;;;;;;;;;;;;;;;;

;; ensure that compressed file extension is gz
gpg  -o - -c aa.flv |gzip -c  | gzip > ax.gz
gzip -cd ax.gz |gzip -cd | gpg -o - -d | vlc -

;;;;;;;;;;;;;;;;;; ok ;;;;;;;;;;;;;;;;

;; ensure that compressed file extension is gz
gpg  -o - -c aa.flv | gzip -c | gzip -c | gzip -c  | gzip > ax.gz
gzip -cd ax.gz | gzip -cd |  gzip -cd | gzip -cd | gpg -o - -d | vlc -

;;;;;;;;;;;;;;;;;; ok ;;;;;;;;;;;;;;;;

error ==> this is not work correctly, there is an error here

gzip -cd ax.gz | gpg -o - -d |  gzip -cd |  gpg -o - -d | vlc -

;;;;;;;;;;;;;;;;;;;;;;;;;;;;;;;;;;;;;;;;;;;;;;;;;;;;;;;;;;;;;;;;


;;;;;  use gpg password as argument ;;;;;;;;
gpg2 version is
gpg --decrypt --batch --passphrase 'original passwd' example.gpg  | gpg --symmetric -o new_example.gpg

gpg1 version is
gpg -d --no-use-agent --passphrase 'original passwd' example.gpg  | gpg -co new_example.gpg

;;;; encrypt then compress twice and use password as argument ;;;;;;;;;;

gpg --no-use-agent --passphrase 'aaabbbccc' -o - -c aa.flv | gzip -c   | gpg --no-use-agent --passphrase 'aaabbbccc'   -o - -c | gzip  > ax.gz
gzip -cd ax.gz | gpg --no-use-agent --passphrase 'aaabbbccc'  -o - -d  |  gzip -cd | gpg --no-use-agent --passphrase 'aaabbbccc'  -o - -d | vlc -



;;use it with for loop by

for f in *.aaa ; do
gpg --no-use-agent --passphrase 'ahmad'  -o "$f .bbb" -d $f
done

or

#!/bin/sh
echo -n "enter  password : "
read  p
for f in *.aaa  ; do
   gpg --no-use-agent --passphrase $p  -o "$f .bbb" -d $f
done

;;;;;;;;;;;;;;;;;;;;;;;;;;;;;;;;;;;;;;;;;;;;;;;;;;;;;;;;;;;;;;;;

;;;; encrypt then compress then encrypt then compress but password prombet
#!/bin/sh
echo -n "enter  password1 : "
read  p1
echo -n "enter  password2 : "
read  p2
gpg --no-use-agent --passphrase $p1  -o - -c aa.flv | gzip -c   | gpg --no-use-agent --passphrase $p2   -o - -c | gzip  > ax.gz

;;;;;;;;;;;;;;;;;;;;;;;;;;;;;;;;;;;;;;;;;;;;;;;;;;;;;;;;;;;;;;;;

;;;; decrypt then decompress then decrypt then decompress but password prombet
#!/bin/sh
echo -n "enter  password2 :  "
read  p2
echo -n "enter  password1 :  "
read  p1
gzip -cd ax.gz | gpg --no-use-agent --passphrase $p2  -o - -d  |  gzip -cd | gpg --no-use-agent --passphrase $p1  -o - -d | vlc -

===================================
jpg --> txt
rename 's/.jpg/.txt/' *
===================================
txt --> jpg
rename 's/.txt/.jpg/' *
===================================
encrypt /decrypt  file
gpg -c filename
gpg filename.gpg
===================================
encrypt /decrypt dir
gpg-zip -c -o file.gpg dirname
gpg-zip -d file.gpg
===================================
pass paaword as argument by this command
echo mypassword |gpg --passphrase-fd 0  -o newFile -d thisFile
for tty problem

decrypt
echo mypassword | gpg --passphrase-fd 0  --no-tty  -o newfile -d thisfile

encrypt
echo mypassword | gpg --passphrase-fd 0  --no-tty  -o newfile -c thisfile


look at this in the future :-

read -sp "Enter passphrase: " pass
echo "${pass}" | gpg --batch --no-tty --yes --passphrase-fd 0 --symmetric -o /path/to/saved/file.jpg.gpg /path/to/file.jpg
echo "${pass}" | gpg --batch --no-tty --yes --passphrase-fd 0 --decrypt -o /path/to/decrypted/file.jpg /path/to/encrypted/file.jpg.gpg

=== fsprotect ===
البرنامج الوحيد في اللنكس الذي يقوم بعمل تجميد للنظام كما يفعل الديب فريز في الوندوز  هو برنامج
fsprotect
وهو يعمل بنفس مبدأ عمل التوزيعات الحية.
المهم لتنزيل البرنامج تقوم بما يلي
apt-get install aufs-tools
apt-get install fsprotect
ثم نقوم بتجميد (ايقاف) البارتشن الروت
وذلك بالتعديل على الملف التالي
/etc/default/grub
نقوم بحذف السطر الاول واضافة السطر الثاني.
والافضل هو عمل كومنت للسطر الاول بدلا من حذفه. كما يلي 
# GRUB_CMDLINE_LINUX_DEFAULT="quiet"    
  GRUB_CMDLINE_LINUX_DEFAULT="quiet splash fsprotect=auto"
  
في هذه الجالة سيقوم البرنامج بحجز نصف ذاكرة (الرام +السواب ) لاجل ان يعمل
البرنامج بشكل جيد.
ثم نعد بعمل تحديث للبوت باستخدام الامر
update-grub
ثم بعد ذلك نقوم بعمل اعادة تشغيل للحاسوب
====================================
كيف اعرف ان برنامج التجميد شعال الان ؟
نكتب الامر
df -h
اذا كان احد البارتشن هكذا
/fsprotect/system
فهذا يعني ان البرنامج شغال وفعال حاليا.
====================================
كيف اقوم بايقاف برنامج التجميد ؟
هناك حلان
الحل الاول :-تشغيل الحاسوب ثم اختيار
- advanced options for linux
- recovery mode
ثم ادخل الى نظام اللنكس ستجد ان برنامج التجميد قد توقف عن العمل .
ولكن برنامج التجميد سيعود الى العمل اذا اعدت تشغيل الجهاز .
---------------
الحل الثاني:-تشغيل الحاسوب ثم اختيار
- advanced options for linux
- recovery mode
ثم نعدل الملف
/etc/default/grub
ونعيده على حاله سابقا او نقلب الكومنت بين السطرين هكذا
  GRUB_CMDLINE_LINUX_DEFAULT="quiet"    
#  GRUB_CMDLINE_LINUX_DEFAULT="quiet splash fsprotect=auto"

ثم نعد بعمل تحديث للبوت باستخدام الامر
update-grub
ثم نعمل اعادة تشغيل للحاسوب
وبهذه الطريقة سيتوقف برنامج التجميد بشكل دائم .
====================================
س :- كيف اقوم بتجميد بارتشن مثل الهوم
/home as seperated partition
ولاحظ ان الهوم هو بارتشن مفصول عن البارتشن الروت. اما لو كان الهوم عندك تحت الروت فلا داع لذلك.

الجواب :- 
نقوم بالتعديل على هذا الملف اذا اردنا ان نجمد بارتشن  غير الروت.
/etc/default/fsprotect
ونضيف اي بارتشن فيه
====================================

protect disk by fsprotect not lethe not not not lethe
apt-get install aufs-tools
apt-get install fsprotect


;;; for protect  file system in another partithon like  /home but   not /
emacs /etc/default/fsprotect

;;; for root system and sub  means / and all sub foluders
;;; warrning => dont use 30% percent, use 5G , if you use 30% means /temp and / will be 1.5 GB
emacs /etc/default/grub
modify this line
# GRUB_CMDLINE_LINUX_DEFAULT="quiet"
  GRUB_CMDLINE_LINUX_DEFAULT="quiet splash fsprotect=5G"

# to change image
GRUB_BACKGROUND="/boot/grub/aa.jpg"

then  then then  write command
update-grub

# note :- fsprotect using the swap, so decrese the swappiness from 60 to 20 ==>(60 means that start using swap when the ram fulled by 40%)
  show the swappiness value by command
  cat /proc/sys/vm/swappiness  ==> must be 20 not 60
  
  to modify  swappiness from 60 to 20 (60 means that start using swap when the ram fulled by 40%)
  1- emacs /etc/sysctl.d/99-sysctl.conf
  2- add this value
     means dont use swap unitl RAM is filled
     vm.swappiness=0
  3- reboot 


  in fedora
  cat /proc/sys/vm/swappiness  
  /etc/sysctl.conf
   vm.swappiness=5
   reboot

or stop the swap by
swapoff  -v /dev/sdb7
or block the swap by
/etc/fstab then remove the swap of hdd (to block partitions )
lsblk -fs ==> to view the uuid


Q:how calculate fsprotect size = 5G ??
ram+swap = 10G (command free -h), then half of it = 5G =>> fsprotect=5G
note :- ram+swap =10G then  ==> fsprotect=5G
note :- 5G from ram+swap (free -mh)
note :- auto ==> 50% of tmpfs files , df -h

================== remap usb keyboard ==============================================

and replace "toshiba" instead of "USB"

http://superuser.com/questions/760602/how-to-remap-keys-under-linux-for-a-specific-keyboard-only
https://lampjs.wordpress.com/tag/linux-2/

i==> keyboard number

apt-get install xinput
apt-get install x11-utils ;; install setxkbmap and xev commands
apt-get install setxkbmap
apt-get install xev

begin script from here

remote_id=$(
    xinput list |
    sed -n 's/.*USB.*id=\([0-9]*\).*keyboard.*/\1/p'
)
[ "$remote_id" ] || exit

#
# remap the following keys, only for my custom vintage atari joystick connected
# through an old USB keyboard:
#
#
# comp =>menu
#
# xkb_symbols "local"
#
#

mkdir -p /tmp/xkb/symbols
cat >/tmp/xkb/symbols/custom <<\EOF
xkb_symbols "remote" {

    key <COMP> { [ Alt_R,          Meta_R ]       };
    key <RWIN> { [ Alt_R,          Meta_R ]       };
    key <RALT> { [ Control_R              ]       };
    key <LALT> { [ Control_L              ]       };
    key <LWIN> { [ Alt_L,          Meta_L ]       };
    key <LCTL> { [ Caps_Lock              ]       };
    key <CAPS> { [ Alt_L,          Meta_L ]       };
};
EOF
setxkbmap -device $remote_id -print | sed 's/\(xkb_symbols.*\)"/\1+custom(remote)"/' | xkbcomp -I/tmp/xkb -i $remote_id -synch - $DISPLAY 2>/dev/null

myFunx1 (){
remote_id=$(
    xinput list |
    sed -n 's/.*GASIA.*id=\([0-9]*\).*keyboard.*/\1/p'
)
[ "$remote_id" ] || exit
# remap the following keys, only for my custom vintage atari joystick connected
# through an old USB keyboard:
# fk1 means f1 , fk12 means f12
#
mkdir -p /tmp/xkb/symbols
cat >/tmp/xkb/symbols/custom <<\EOF
 xkb_symbols "remote" {
 #    key <COMP> { [ Alt_R,          Meta_R ]       };
 #    key <RWIN> { [ Alt_R,          Meta_R ]       };
 #    key <RALT> { [ Control_R              ]       };
 #    key <LALT> { [ Control_L              ]       };
 #    key <RALT> { [ Control_L              ]       };
 #    key <RALT> { [ space                  ]       };
 #    key <RALT> { [ NoSymbol,   Control_L  ]       };
 #    key  <ALT> { [ NoSymbol,        Alt_L ]       };
 #    key <LWIN> { [ Alt_L,          Meta_L ]       };
 #    key <LCTL> { [ Caps_Lock              ]       };
      key <CAPS> { [ Alt_L,          Meta_L ]       };
      key <FK01> { [ x                      ]       };
      key <FK12> { [ x                      ]       };
};
EOF
setxkbmap  -layout us,ara  -option grp:shift_toggle
setxkbmap  -device $remote_id    -option altwin:ctrl_alt_win  -print | sed 's/\(xkb_symbols.*\)"/\1+custom(remote)"/' | xkbcomp -I/tmp/xkb -i $remote_id -synch - $DISPLAY 2>/dev/null
}
alias usbk='myFunx1'

# put it in .bashrc by function
# setxkbmap -device $remote_id -print | sed 's/\(xkb_symbols.*\)"/\1+custom(remote)"/' | xkbcomp -I/tmp/xkb -i $remote_id -synch - $DISPLAY 2>/dev/null
# save it in bash file then install xinput command
# apt-get install xinput
# to view all keys  xkbcomp -i 15 $DISPLAY /home/myusbkblayout.xkb

#  build  website by apache on my laptop
1- open router then DMZ
   incomming port 8888 // means the website port like yhaoo.8888
   forward port 8888 // means forwarding the incomming port to the forward port, that means the apache port
2- add the apache port 8888 to /etc/apache2/ports.conf add =>  Listen 8888
service apache2 start  // run apache service
apache2ctl start         // run apache website in this path /var/www/html
3- notice that permision will be
   folder html ==>> chmod 755 html          ==>    rwxr-xr-x
   inside html folder ==> chmod 744 html/*  ==>    rwxr--r--
4- run firewall by command gufw then modify it like this
incomming deny // means connections from internet to my computer throw the ports 8888 ==>> add runle for allowing  in(incoomming ) for port 8888 only
outgoing allow // menas connections from my computer to the internet so all ports for visiting websites will be avialable
iptables -I INPUT -p tcp --dport 8888 -j ACCEPT -m comment --comment "Allow HTTP"

5-for monitoring who is visiting my website by
ss -pn | grep :8888
watch -n 5  "ss -pn | grep :8888"
watch -n 5 "netstat -n  | grep :8888"
or or or or
by this log file
/var/log/apache2/other_vhosts_access.log
note:-
you can use tor or proxy with DMZ if you have one internet router

How to Password Protect Web Directories in Apache Using .htaccess File
http://www.tecmint.com/password-protect-apache-web-directories-using-htaccess/

---------------- On RedHat/CentOS based systems ----------------
# vi /etc/httpd/conf/httpd.conf
---------------- On Debian/Ubuntu based systems ----------------
# nano /etc/apache2/sites-available/000-default.conf



When you manage online projects, you often need to limit access to that project in order to protect it against the outside world. There are might be different reasons for that – for example you want to prevent search engine crawlers from accessing your site while it is still in development phase.
Password Protect Apache Web Directories
Password Protect Apache Web Directories
In this tutorial, I am going to show you how to password protected different web sites directories in Apache web server. There are many ways you can achieve this, but we will review two of them which are most commonly used.
The first method configures password protection directly in Apache’s configuration file, while the second one uses .htaccess file.
Requirements
In order to setup password protection for your web directories, you will need to have:
    A working Apache web server
    The AllowOverride AuthConfig directive must be enabled in Apache configuration file.
Setup Apache Password Protected Directory
1. For this tutorial, we will be protecting the main web root directory /var/www/html.  To protect that directory, open your Apache’s configuration:
---------------- On RedHat/CentOS based systems ----------------
# vi /etc/httpd/conf/httpd.conf
---------------- On Debian/Ubuntu based systems ----------------
# nano /etc/apache2/sites-available/000-default.conf
2. Find the Apache Document directory root for /var/www/html and add the following things as suggested:
On Apache 2.2 Version
<Directory /var/www/html>
Options Indexes Includes FollowSymLinks MultiViews
AllowOverride All
allow,deny
Allow from all
</Directory>
On Apache 2.4 Version
<Directory /var/www/html>
Options Indexes Includes FollowSymLinks MultiViews
AllowOverride All
Require all granted
</Directory>


3. Save the file and restart Apache by using the following command:
--------------- On Systemd -------------------
# systemctl restart httpd         [On RedHat based systems]
# systemctl restart apache2       [On Debian based systems]
--------------- On SysV init -----------------
# service httpd restart           [On RedHat based systems]
# service apache2 restart         [On Debian based systems]
4. Now we will use the htpasswd command to generate username and password for our protected directory. This command is used to manage user files for basic authentication.
The general syntax of the command is:
# htpasswd -c filename username
The -c option specifies the file that will keep the encrypted password and username specifies the user for the authentication.
5. Our password file needs to be located out of the Apache’s web accessible directory so that it is well protected. For that purpose, we will create new directory:
# mkdir /home/tecmint
6. After that we will generate our username and password that will be stored in that directory:
# htpasswd -c /home/tecmint/webpass tecmint
Once you execute this command you will have to enter a password for our new user "tecmint" twice:
this command

After that we will need to make sure that Apache is able to read the “webpass” file. For that purpose, you will need to change the ownership of that file with the following command:
---------------- On RedHat/CentOS based systems ----------------
# chown apache: /home/tecmint/webpass
# chmod 640 /home/tecmint/webpass
---------------- On Debian/Ubuntu based systems ----------------
# chown www-data /home/tecmint/webpass
# chmod 640 /home/tecmint/webpass
7. At this point our new user and password are ready. Now we need to tell Apache to request password when accessing our targeted directory. For that purpose, create file called .htaccess in /var/www/html:
# vi /var/www/html/.htaccess
Add the following code in it:
AuthType Basic
AuthName "Restricted Access"
AuthUserFile /home/tecmint/webpass
Require user tecmint

8. Now save the file and put your setup to the test. Open your browser and enter your IP address or domain name in the web browser, for example:
http://ip-address
You should be prompted for username and password:

;;;;;;;;;;;;;;;;;;;;;;;;;;;;;;;;;;;;;;;;;;;;;;;;

# How to Encrypt and Decrypt Files and Directories Using Tar and OpenSSL
# encrypt and decrypt
tar -czf - * | openssl enc -e -aes256 -out secured.tar.gz
openssl enc -d -aes256 -in secured.tar.gz | tar xz -C test

;;;;;;;;;;;;;;;;;;;;;;;;;;;;;;;;;;;;;;;;;;;;;;;;;;;;;;;;;;;;;;;;
what is mean of 2>&1
1>  File descriptor 1 is the standard output (stdout).
2>  File descriptor 2 is the standard error (stderr).
2>&1 means  redirect stderr to stdout
;;;;;;;;;;;;;;;;;;;;;;;;;;;;;;;;;;;;;;;;;;;;;;;;;;;;;;;;;;;;;;;;
;; find mac address by airodump-ng by this command only
airodump-ng wlan0mon 2>&1 | grep -o  "amam" 2>&1
airodump-ng wlan0mon 2>&1 | grep -q "84:A6:C8:1C:B6:78" ;  speaker-test -t sine -f 1000 -l 1 ; xmessage  -center  "found at $(date)"
-o means display only amam
-q exit when match mac

[[[ backup backup backup backup backup backup ]]]

fdisk -l
df -Th

# partition to partiton
dd if=/dev/sda of=/dev/sdb
use bs to increase the speed
dd if=/dev/sda of=/dev/sdb bs=100M

# partition to partiton, no errors
dd if=/dev/sda of=/dev/sdb conv=noerror,sync

# partition to image in harddisk, then restore it
dd if=/dev/hda of=~/hdadisk.img
dd if=hdadisk.img of=/dev/hda

# from cd to iso
dd if=/dev/cdrom of=tgsservice.iso bs=2048

# from iso to usb
dd if=kali-linux-1.0.9a-amd64.iso of=/dev/sdb bs=512k




[[[final  my backup ]]], must compress it to be reduce the size. by gzip, please visit the below url
https://wiki.archlinux.org/index.php/disk_cloning


;;;;;;;;;;;;;;;;


use iso not img, so can open it temp by mount iso as above
always use bs speed bs=100 to increase speed when copying the data

partions are boot(sda1), home(sda5) /home,      root(sda7) /,
dd if=/dev/sda1 of=/media/root/hitachi/backup/partition_backup/myBoot.iso bs=100M
dd if=/dev/sda5 of=/media/root/hitachi/backup/partition_backup/MyHome.iso bs=100M
dd if=/dev/sda7 of=/media/root/hitachi/backup/partition_backup/MyRoot.iso bs=100M
# to restore
dd if=/media/root/hitachi/backup/partition_backup/myBoot.iso   of=/dev/sda1 bs=100M
dd if=/media/root/hitachi/backup/partition_backup/MyHome.iso   of=/dev/sda5 bs=100M
dd if=/media/root/hitachi/backup/partition_backup/MyRoot.iso   of=/dev/sda7 bs=100M

--backup boot--
sda means all the partitions sda1,sda2,sda3,sda4,sda5,,,,,so dont play with it ,copy just first 512 byte onle once(count =1)
dd if=/dev/sda  of=/home/myboot/boot1.iso bs=512 count=1
dd if=/dev/sda1 of=/home/myboot/boot2.iso bs=512 count=1
dd if=/dev/sda1 of=/home/myboot/boot3.iso
--restore boot--
means copy only 512 byte only once to sda
dd if=/home/myboot/boot1.iso of=/dev/sda  bs=512 count=1

dd if=/home/myboot/boot2.iso of=/dev/sda1 bs=512 count=1
dd if=/home/myboot/boot3.iso of=/dev/sda1
or or or or or
or by using dvd repair boot from my dvd

[[not work]]
[[dont use it]]
[[why]]
 because there is no defragment in linux so, may be you will copy empty data
[[[[ small image partion ]]]]
[[[[dd dd dd dd dd dd dd  to make partion.img is small by dd dd dd dd dd ]]]]
very important notes of dd dd dd dd
to copy used partion, not empty data partion
if i need copy only first 1GB of partiton because the the partion have 7G empty(not used ) and 1G used
df -Th, df -T  df  ==> to see the size
so to copy used partion,not empty, i need to specifty the used data by df -Th
dd if=/dev/sda5 of=just1GB.img  bs=1G count=1

so  it is very easy just 3 steps

command => df -Th, df -Th, df -T , df
Filesystem     Type      Size  Used Avail Use% Mounted on
/dev/sda7      ext4       37G   11G   24G  32% /fsprotect/system
/dev/sda5      ext4       28G  7.2G   19G  28% /home

1- first need check  data in partion
DO NOT RUN THIS ON A MOUNTED PARTITION! It can seriously damage your filesystem.
sudo fsck.ext4 -fn /dev/sda5
sudo fsck.ext4 -fn /dev/sda7
there is no defragment in linux so, may be you will copy empty data


2- copy only used data, not empty partion , always add additional 1G, use command
df wihtout any arguement
dd if=/dev/sda5 of=sda5_8G.img    bs=8G count=1
dd if=/dev/sda7 of=sda7_12G.img  bs=12G count=1

3- need to restore partions
dd  if=sda5_8G.img  of=/dev/sda5   bs=8G count=1
dd  if=sda7_12G.img of=/dev/sda7   bs=12G count=1
